dhāiẏā āhilā nikaṭera bhaktagaṇa ||1658||  

āra yata loka āise kahe paraspare |  
iki gaṇḍagola śuni nadīẏā-nagare ||1659||  

aiche kahi prabhura e bhavane āśiẏā |  
haẏena mohita prabhupāne nirakhiẏā ||1660||  

adbhuta prabhura nṛtya, kīrtana, pracāra |  
ithe kona jana dhairya nāre, dharivāra ||1661||  

prabhu-premāveśa dekhi cinte sarvajana |  
prabhuke karilā sthira prabhu-bhaktagaṇa ||1662||  

ohe bāpa śrīnivāsa, viśvambhara ethā |  
āpanāre prakāśaẏe e adbhuta kathā ||1663||  

bhaktādhīna prabhu, bhakta-duḥkha-nāśa haẏa |  
pāṣaṇḍīra prati krodha haila atiśaẏa ||1664||  

mui sei, mui sei baliẏā baliẏā |  
hāse, kānde, mahā-ghora huṅkāra kariẏā ||1665||  

dekhiẏā pāṣaṇḍigaṇa khedār̤iẏā yāẏa |  
darpa kari, kahe saṁhārimu to sabhāẏa ||1666||  

kṣaṇe bhūme loṭāiẏā thira haiẏā rahe |  
aiche dekhi keha keha āi-prati kahe ||1667||  

pūrvavāyubala ebe karila im̐hāre |  
karaha śaityaka sevā aśeṣa prakāre ||1668||  

lokadvāre āi jānāila śrīnivāse |  
tem̐ha prabodhila ati manera ullāse ||1669||  

sakalei kahe e manuṣya kabhu naẏa |  
haïlena vyakta ethā śācīra tanaẏa ||1670||  

śuna śrīnivāsa, eka divasera kathā |  
premāveśe atyanta vihvala prabhu ethā ||1671||  

yāre dekhe tāre puche kṛṣṇa kon khāle ? |  
nivārite nāre vāridhārā dunaẏane ||1672||  

gadādhara tāmbūla laïẏā āilā ethā |  
tām̐re puche śyāmala sundara kṛṣṇa kothā ||1673||  

tem̐ho kahe, sadā kṛṣṇa hṛdaẏe tomāra |  
śuni nakhe hṛdaẏa ciraẏe āpanāra ||1674||  

prabhu duikare śīghra dhare gadādhara |  
kata prabodhila sthira haila viśvambhara ||1675||  

gadādhare mahātuṣṭa haiẏā kahe āi |  
nimāira saṅge bāpa rāhibe sadāi ||1676||  

ethā sandhyākāle āsi mile bhaktagaṇa |  
mukunda par̤aẏe śloka ati rasāẏana ||1677||  

bhaktirasamaẏa śloka śuni gaurarāẏa |  
ye prema-āveśa tāhā kahā nāi yāẏa ||1678||  

vaiṣṇava-veṣṭita prabhu matta saṁkīrtane |  
haila kṣaṇaprāẏa niśi prabhāta nā jāne ||1679||  

premānande huṅkāra-garjana atiśaẏa |  
śuni pāṣaṇḍīra rātre nidrā nāi haẏa ||1680||  

karaẏe vidrūpa krodhe pāṣaṇḍīra gaṇa |  
keha kahe āji e sabhāra vir̤ambana ||1681||  

nadīẏāẏa kīrtana, e amaṅgala ithe |  
āise rājāra loka vaiṣṇave dharite ||1682||  

e sabhe pālābe jāni hao sāvadhāna |  
śrīvāse bām̐dhiẏā dile sabhāra kalyāṇa ||1683||  

śrīvāsa udāra śuni karila pratyaẏa |  
duṣṭa, rājā yavana asādhya kichu naẏa ||1684||  

eta vicāriẏā śrīvāsera bhaẏa haila |  
antaryāmī viśvambhara sakala jānila ||1685||  

huṅkāra kariẏā prabhu kahe vāra vāra |  
bhaktabhaẏa vināśite mora avatāra ||1686||  

prabhu avatīrṇa ihā bhakte nāi jāne |  
āpanāre prakāśite icchā haila mane ||1687||  

kariẏā suveśa prabhu ulasita cite |  
nadīẏā-bhramaṇe raṅge cale ethā haite ||1688||  

se rūpa-lāvaṇī dekhi kebā thira haẏa |  
manera ullāse keu kāre kata kaẏa ||1689||  

tathāhi—gīte  
dekha bhuvanamohana gorā nadīẏānagare |  
rūpera chaṭāẏa daśadiśā ālo kare || dhru ||1690||  

kunakabhūṣara garavabhañjana, mañju mūrati rasāla re |  
kuṭila kuntala vimala malaẏaja, tilaka jhalakata bhāli re ||1691||  

atanu-dhanu dūre, darapa bhurudiṭhi, bhaṅgi ki madhura bhām̐tiẏā |  
hāsamilita maẏaṅka mukhalasa, daśana motima pām̐tiẏalā ||1692||  

cāru śruti avataṁsa sundara, gaṇḍamaṇḍala śohaẏe |  
nāsikā śuṣka-cañcu jiti, satī yuvatīgaṇa-mana mohaẏe ||1693||  

jānu lambita, lalita bhujayuga, gañji bhujaga mṛṇāla re |  
vakṣa parisara parama sugaṭhana, kaṇṭhe mālatī-māla re ||1694||  

trinvali-balita, sunābhi sarasija, bhramara tanuruha rājaẏe |  
siṁha jini kaṭi-deśa kṛśa ghana, aṁśu aṁśuka bhrājaẏe ||1695||  

madana-mada dali, kadali uru uru, parva ati anupāma re |  
caraṇatala khala-kamala-nakhamaṇi-nichani ghana ghanaśyāma re ||1696||  

kebā nā bhulaẏe gorācānde nirakhiẏā |  
ei pathe calilena bhramite nadīẏā ||1697||  

nadīẏā-bhramaṇe prabhu śrīvāsera ghare |  
hailā caturbhuja kṛpā kari śrīvāsere ||1698||  

āsi viprasaṅge basilā ethāi |  
se adbhuta śobhāra upamā dite nāi ||1699||  

eikhāne prabhura adbhuta bhāvāveśa |  
kṛṣṇa bali kāndaẏe dhairyera nāhi leśa ||1700||  

ekkadina varāhabhāvete matta hailā |  
ethā haite murāriguptera ghara gelā ||1701||  

haïẏā varāhamūrti tām̐re kṛpā kari |  
ethāi āsiẏā basilena gaurahari ||1702||  

laïẏā sakala bhakte prabhu vilasaẏa |  
eka nityānanda vinu vyākula hṛdaẏa ||1703||  

ohe śrīnivāsa, nityānanda haladhara |  
hār̤āi paṇḍita padmāvatīra kumāra ||1704||  

sarvapūjya hār̤āi paṇḍita, padmāvatī |  
rār̤hadeśe ekacakrā grāmete vasati ||1705||  

parama udāra dui brāhmaṇa-brāhmaṇī |  
apāra mahimā guṇa kahite nā jāni ||1706||  

prabhu nityānanda sukha dite sarvajane |  
tām̐ra ghare avatīrṇa hailā śubhakṣaṇe ||1707||  

nityānandaprabhu-janmatithi vilakṣaṇa |  
ke vā nā ārādhe ke nā karaẏe vandana ||1708||  

tathāhi—  
sarvamaṅgalarūpāḥ tāṁ māghaśuklatraẏodaśīm |  
nityānandaprabhorjanmatithiṁ vande mudāniśam ||1709||  

prabhu-janmakāle ye ānanda upajila |  
tāhā vijñagaṇa nānāprakāre varṇila ||1710||  

gīte yathā—kāmoda—  

āhā mari āju ki ānanda |  
kibā ekacakrāpure,		hār̤āi paṇḍitera ghare,  
avatīrṇa hailā nityānanda || dhrru ||1711||  

ati sukomala tanu,		hema navalīta janu,  
śobhāẏa bhuvana vimohita |  
putramukha nirakhiẏā,	ulāse nā dhare hiẏā,  
padmāvatī hār̤āi paṇḍita ||1712||  

śrīadvaita śāntipure,		garjaẏe ānandabhare,  
tileka haïte nāre thira |  
nāce prabhu ūrdhvabāhe,	kām̐khatālī diẏā kahe,  
‘ānilu ānilu balavīra’ ||1713||  

brahmā ādi devagaṇa,		kare puṣpa-variṣaṇa,  
aẏa jaẏa-dhvani anivāra |  
gandharva kinnara yata,		vāẏa vādya kata śata,  
gāẏa guṇa sukhera pāthāra ||1714||  

ojhā mahābhāgyavān,		putrera kalyāṇe dāna,  
kare yata lekhā nāi dite |  
kata nā yautuka laiẏā,		loka saba āse dhāẏā,  
mahābhir̤a gṛhe praveśite ||1715||  

dhanya rār̤ha, mahī āra,		dhanya se nakṣatra vāra,  
dhanya māgha-śukla traẏodaśī |  
nara hari kahe bhāla,		dhanya dhanya kalikāla,  
prakaṭe khaṇṭila duḥkharāśi ||1716||  

punaḥ—suhaï—  

prabhu nityānanda,	ānandera kanda,  
pūrabe rohiṇītanaẏa yem̐ho |  
dhanya kali kailā,		śubhakṣaṇe hailā,  
padmāvatīgarbhe prakaṭa tem̐ho ||1717||  

jaẏa jaẏa jaẏa,		dhvani atiśaẏa,  
maṅgala hār̤āi paṇḍita-ghare |  
ekacakrāvāsī,		loka sukhe bhāsi  
dhāẏā āse dhṛti dharite nāre ||1718||  

sutikā-māndire,		jhalamala kare,  
nitāira sukhacandramā cāru |  
se śobhā dekhite,		kata sādha cite,  
dekhe, ām̐khi nāi nimikha kāru ||1719||  


harṣe devagaṇa,		varṣe puṣpa ghana,  
alakhita nṛtya-bhaṅgimā bhāle |  
ghanaśyāma gāẏa,	nānā vādya vāẏa,  
dhā dhā dhiki dhiki, dhennā nā tāle ||1720||  

nityānanda-janma bālya-līlā manohara |  
gṛhe vāsa kailā prabhu dvādaśa vatsara ||1721||  

sannyāsīra chale gṛha haïte calilā |  
tīrthaparyaṭana kare e adbhuta līlā ||1722||  

sarvamanoratha-siddhi kari paryaṭane |  
prabhura prakāśa lāgi rahe bvṛndāvane ||1723||  

guptarūpe nadīẏā vihāre gauracandra |  
haïlā prakāśa tā jānilā nityānanda ||17 24||  

mahā-premānande matta haiẏā nirantara |  
āilena navadvīpe deva haladhara ||1725||  

nandana ācārya-gṛhe gamana kārilā |  
tem̐ho mahāteja dekhi adhairya haïlā ||1726||  

mahāyatne nityānanda candre rākhi ghare |  
karāila bhikṣā ati ullāsa antara ||1727||  

nityānanda-gamana jāniẏā gaurarāẏa |  
manda manda hāse mahā ullāsa hiẏāẏa ||1728||  

e viṣṇu-mandire viṣṇu pūje viśvambhara |  
ethāi vaiṣṇava saba mililā satvara ||1729||  

se śobhā dekhiẏā prabhu ullasita mane |  
rajanī-svapana-kathā kahe eikhāne ||1730||  

gīte yathā—kāmoda—  

prabhu viśvambhara,	priẏa parikara  
prati kahe śuna svapana-kathā |  
kibā se nirmita,		ati suśobhita,  
āladhvaja ratha āila ethā ||1731||  

dekhinu sundara,		dīrgha kalevara,  
puruṣa eka ki upamā tāhe |  
eka karṇe kibā,		kuṇḍala se grībā,  
kibā mukhaśaśī bhubvana mohe ||1732||  

kāla kumbha hāte,		līla vastra māthe,  
nīla vāsa paridhāna suchānde |  
caudige nehāle,		heli duli cale,  
se bhaṅgite kebā dhairaya bāndhe ||1733||  

mora nāma dhari		puche beri beri,  
bujhi haladhara gamana kailā |  
eta kāhi nara-		hari prabhuvara,  
balarāma-bhāve vihvala hailā ||1734||  

śrīvāsādi prabhu svapnāveśe nirakhiẏā |  
karilena stuti sabe susthira haïẏā ||1735||  

viśvambhara-ceṣṭā kichu kahila nā haẏa |  
dekhite nitāicānde utkṣaṇṭhātiśaẏa ||1736||  

haridāsa śrīāvāsapaṇḍite kichu kaiẏā |  
nityānanda aṇveṣaṇe dila pāṭhāiẏā ||1737||  

haridāsa, śrīvāsa sarvāṁśe vicakṣaṇa |  
navadvīpe prati ghare kaila anveṣaṇa ||1738||  

kothāo nā pāiẏā kahaẏe prabhupāśe |  
śuni prabhu kahi kata manda manda hāse ||1739||  

prabhura e bhaṅgi kichu anye nā jānila |  
nityānanda parama durjñeẏa jānāila ||1740||  

śobhāmaẏa apūrva suveśe gauracandra |  
priẏagaṇa-saṅge cale yathā nityānanda ||1741||  

mili nityānande rākhi śrībvāsera ghare |  
ethā āsi baise prabhu ullāsa antare ||1742||  

śrīvāsera gṛha heaite rāmāi āsiẏā |  
nityānanda-ceṣṭā kahe ethāẏa basiẏā ||1743||  

punaḥ punaḥ puche prabhu kaha tām̐ra rīta |  
prabhu-āge kahe kichu rāmāi paṇḍita ||1744||  

katho rātre nityānanda kariẏā huṅkāra |  
bhāṅgi phele daṇḍa kamaṇḍalu āpanāra ||1745||  

śuni prabhu viśvambhara īṣat hāsiẏā |  
śrīvāsera gṛhe gelā ei patha diẏā ||1746||  

ohe śrīnibvāsa nija-gṛhe ye kautuka |  
tāhā ki baliba sabe mora eka mukha ||1747||  

ekadina eikhāne prabhu gaurarāẏa |  
bhaktagaṇa madhye baise vihvala premāẏa ||1748||  

kahi kata śrīadvaita ācārya ānite |  
pāṭhāilā śāntipure śrīrāmapaṇḍite ||1749||  

śāsntipure advaitera bvāsa ye prakāre |  
śuna śrīnivāsa tāhā kahiẏe tomāre ||1750||  

advaitera pitā pitāmahādi vikhyāta |  
baṅge vāsa pūrve śāntipure gatāẏāta ||1751||  

baṅgadeśe śrīhaṭṭa-nikaṭa navagrāma |  
sarvārādhāya advaitacandrera priẏadhāma ||1752||  

tathā rahe vipra śrīkubera mahāśaẏa |  
miśra paṇḍitācārya e skhyāti tām̐ra haẏa ||1753||  

tem̐ho advaitera pitā tām̐ra śuddha rīta |  
sarvaprakārete yogya sarvatra vidita ||1754||  

tathāhi śrīgauragaṇoddeśadīpikāẏām—  
mahādebvasya mitraṁ yaḥ kubero guhyakeśvaraḥ |  
kuberapaṇḍitaḥ so’dya janako’sya vidāmbaraḥ ||1755||  

nābhānāme śrīkubera-miśrera gharaṇī |  
ati patitvratā yem̐ho advaita-jananī ||1756||  

putrera kāmanā pūrve dom̐hāra āchila |  
tāhā vṛddhakāle navagrāme pūrṇa haila ||1757||  

navagrāme janmilena śrīadbvaitacandra |  
janmakāle bhuvane vyāpila mahānanda ||1758||  

śrīadvaita-janma-vṛttānta—  

gīte—māura—  

māghe śuklātithi,		saptamīte ati,  
uthalaẏe mahā ānanda-sindhu |  
nābhāgarbha dhanya	kari abvatīrṇa,  
haila śubhakṣaṇe, advaita-indu ||1759||  

kubera paṇḍita		haiẏā haraṣita,  
nānā dāna dvija-daridre diẏā |  
sūtikā-mandire,		giẏā dhīre dhīre,  
dekhi putramukha jur̤āẏa hiẏā ||1760||  

navagrāmavāsī,		loka dhāẏā āsi  
paraspara kahe nā dekhi hena |  
kibā puṇyaphale,		miśra vṛddhakāle  
pāilena putraratana yena ||1761||  

puṣpa-variṣaṇa,		kare suragaṇa,  
alakṣita rīti upamā nahu |  
jaẏa jaẏa-dhvani,		bharala avanī,  
bhane ghanaśyāma maṅgala bahu ||1762||  

punaḥ—bhūpālī—  

māgha-saptamī		śuklapakṣa,  
śubhakṣaṇa kṣaṇa bhūri |  
prakaṭi prabhu,		advaita sundara,  
karala kulimada dūri ||1763||  

dhāi calu saba,		loka pauṭhi,  
kurera-bhavana-mājhāra |  
vipula pulaka,		viloki bālaka,  
deta jaẏā jaẏakāra ||1764||  

bhāṭagaṇa ghana,		bhaṇata yaśa,  
gāẏata guṇī muda māti |  
sughara vādaka		vṛnda vāẏata,  
vādya kata kata bhām̐ti ||1765||  

karata nartaka,		nṛtya ughaṭate,  
thaitā taka taka thona |  
dāsa narahari		pahum̐ka janama,  
vilāsa varaṇaba kona ||1766||  

ohe śrīnivāsa advaitera janmakāle |  
śrīkṛṣṇa govindanāma uccaiḥsvare bale ||1767||  

advaitera bālyalīlā ati rasāẏaṇa |  
janmāẏena sabhāra santoṣa anukṣaṇa ||1768||  

śrīkurera nābhā gaṅgārāsera nimitte |  
āilena śāntipure navagrāma haite ||1769||  

kurera paṇḍita nābhādevī putra laiẏā |  
śāntipure rahe mahā ullasita haiẏā ||1770||  

putre nānā śāstra karāẏā adhyaẏana |  
kathodine dom̐he haïlena adarśana ||1771||  

advaita-īśvara mātā-pitā adarśane |  
gaẏāchale gelā sarvatīrtha-paryaṭane ||1772||  

vṛndāvane kathodina kṛṣṇe ārādhaẏa |  
jānilena navadvīpe prakaṭa samaẏa ||1773||  

vṛndāvana haite prabhu kariẏā gamana |  
gaur̤e āsi kaila gaur̤a baṅgete bhramaṇa ||1774||  

navadvīpa haïẏā āilā śāntipure |  
dekhi śāntipuravāsī ullāsa antare ||1775||  

pūrva haite apūrva ālaẏa kari dila |  
advaita-sevāẏa sabhe niyukta haïla ||1776||  

sarvaśāstre adhyāpaka ādvaita ācārya |  
ke bujhite pāre tām̐ra alaukika kāẏrya ||1777||  

śrīadvaita-ācārya-vivāha karāite |  
viśiṣṭa lokera ceṣṭā haila bhālamate ||1778||  

sakalei kailā vivāhera āẏojalna |  
tāhā jānilena prabhu kurera-nandana ||1779||  

karite vivāha adbvaitera icchā haila |  
manda manda hāsi sabhe anumati dila ||1780||  

sabhe mahāharṣa haiẏa giẏā nija-ghare |  
jānāila nṛsiṁha-bhādur̤‌i vipravare ||1781||  

bhāgyavanta nṛsiṁha viprera dui kanyā |  
vivāhera yogya, rūpe guṇe mahā dhanyā ||1782||  

śrīadvaitaprabhura vivāha—  

nṛsiṁha bhādur̤‌i ati ullāsa antare |  
dui kanyā sampradāna kailā advaitere ||1783||  

advaitera vivāhera sukhera nāi ante |  
bahu artha vyaẏa kaila yata bhāgyavanta ||1784||  

ācāryera bhāryā dui jagat pūjitā |  
sarvatra vidita nāma ‘śrī’ āra ‘sītā’ ||1785||  

tathāhi śrīgaurapgaṇoddeśadīpikāẏām—  
yogamāẏā bhagavatī gṛhiṇī tasya sāmpratam |  
sītārūpeṇāvatīrṇā śrīnāmnī tatprakāśataḥ ||1786||  

sarvatattvajñātā dui advaitagharaṇī |  
dom̐hāra ẏe ceṣṭā tāhā kahite ki jāni ||1787||  

aiche rahe śāntipure śrī advaita rāẏa |  
karilena eka vāsasthāna nadīẏāẏa ||1788||  

prāẏa śrīvāsera gṛhe advaita sthiti |  
kṛṣṇarasāsvāde nā jānaẏe divārāti ||1789||  

kabhu śāntipure, kabhu rahe nadīẏāẏa |  
kṛṣṇavinā kathodina udvege goṅāẏa ||1790||  

kṛṣṇe ārādhaẏe sadā aśeṣa prakāre |  
haïlā prakaṭa kṛṣṇa advaita-huṅkāre ||1791||  

prabhura adbhuta līlā dekhe nadīẏāẏa |  
nā karaẏe vyakta sabhe, prakāre jānāẏa ||1792||  

prabhu prakāśiẏā pūji ullāsa antare |  
kata manoratha kari gelā śāntipure ||1793||  

śrīrāmapaṇḍita giẏā prabhura ājñāẏa |  
prabhu ye kahila tāhā kahila tām̐hāẏa ||17984||  

haïẏā vihvala śrīadvaita premāveśe |  
ye ye kathā kahaẏe tā kahite nā āise ||1795||  

advaita bhavane mahānanda uthalila |  
prabhu-pūjā-dravya sītādevī sajja kaila ||1796||  

advaitera ye kautuka kahane nā yāẏa |  
goṣṭhīsaha advaita āise nadīẏāẏa ||1797||  

advaita āise jāni prabhu gaurahari |  
e pathe śrīvāsa-gṛhe gelā śīghra kari ||1798||  

bhaktagoṣṭhī-sahite śrīgaurāṅgasundara |  
nija-gṛhe saṁkīrtane magna nirantara ||1799||  

ekhā saṅkīrtanānande sthira nāhi bāndhe |  
puṇḍarīka vidyānidhi bali prabhu kānde ||1800||  

kṣaṇe bāpa, kṣaṇe bandhu baliẏā kāndaẏa |  
puṇḍarīka vidyānidhi priẏa atiśaẏa ||1801||  

sarvamate śreṣṭha tām̐ra vāsa baṅgadeśe |  
cakraśālā-nāme grāma cāṭigrāma-pāśe ||1802||  

madhye madhye śrīnavadvīpeo sthiti haẏā |  
navadvīpe āche tām̐ra apūrva āramlaẏa ||1803||  

tem̐ha mahāvaiṣṇava cinite sādhya kāra |  
dekhile viṣaẏī jñāna haẏata sabhāra 1||1804||  

ohe śrīnivāsa, gauracandra nijamukhe |  
kahite caritra tām̐ra bhāse mahāsukhe ||1805||  

prabhu-ākarṣaṇe tem̐ho āilā nadīẏāẏa |  
rātriyoge āśi mile prabhure ethāẏa ||1806||  

ānande mūrchita hailā prabhure dekhiẏā |  
bhāsaẏe netrera jale cetana pāiẏā ||1807||  

karaẏe yateka kheta ye dainya prakāśe |  
dekhite se daśā sabhe netrajale bhāse ||1808||  

vidyānidhi gosāñire prabhu vakṣe dhari |  
haïlena yaiche tāhā kahite nā pāri ||1809||  

sabhāre kahaẏe prabhu ullāsa haïyā |  
dekhilāma premanidhi naẏana bhariẏā ||1810||  

aiche kata kahi prabhu śrīgaurasundara |  
netrajale siñce vidyānidhi-kalevara ||1811||  

vidyānidhi premāẏa vihvala anivāra |  
prabhura icchāẏa bāhyajñāna haila tām̐ra ||1812||  

takhana praṇame prabhu cini āpanāra |  
śrīadvaita ācārye karila namaskāra ||1813||  

yathāyogya milana haïla bhaktasane |  
pāilena parama ānanda bhaktagaṇe ||1814||  

kṣaṇekei premabhakti āvirbhāva haïte |  
haila ye prakāra tāhā nā āise kahite ||1815||  

vidyānidhi mahānande haïẏā vidāẏa |  
ei pathe gelā tem̐ha āpana-vāsāẏa ||1816||  

ohe śrīnivāsa, ekadina śacīmātā |  
dekhila ye svapna tāhā karaẏe putre ethā ||1817||  

putrapāne cāhi āi kahe snehāveśe |  
śuna bāpa, svapne yā dekhilu niśiśeṣe ||1818||  

tumi āra nityānanda kalaha kariẏā |  
viṣṇu-ghare gelā pañcavarṣera haïẏā ||1819||  

gharera bhitare dekhilāma cārijana |  
tumi, nityānanda, kṛṣṇa, rohiṇīnandana ||1820||  

tathā nityānanda kṛṣṇa-haste hasta dilā |  
balarāma-haste tumi hasta āropilā ||1821||  

aiche ghara haite bāhira haiẏā cārijane |  
kailā kata kalaha āmāra vidyamāne ||1822||  

nānā dravya kār̤ākār̤i kariẏā khāilā |  
nityānanda mā baliẏā mora āge āilā ||1823||  

more kahe kṣudhā haila anna deha mātā |  
nidrābhaṅga haila mora śuni ei kathā ||1824||  

jāgiẏā dekhilu niśiprabhāta-samaẏa |  
kichu nā bujhiẏe mora mane kata haẏa ||1825||  

śuni mahānande prabhu manda manda hāse |  
kahi kata māẏe puna kahe mṛdubhāṣe ||1826||  

‘adya nityānande ethā karāha bhojana’ |  
śuni jananīra ati ullasita mana ||1827||  

bhikṣāra sāmagrī śacī śīghra sajja kailā |  
nityānande prabhu mahānande laiẏā āilā ||1828||  

eikhāne āsiẏā basilā duijana |  
ethā baise gadādhara ādi āptagaṇa ||1829||  

ohe śrīnivāsa, se apūrva śobhā heri |  
caraṇa duite jala dilu śīghra kari ||1830||  

karaẏe bhojana dom̐he basiẏā ethāi |  
śyāma śuklarūpa nirikhāẏe śacī āi ||1831||  

dom̐hāra adbhuta śobhā vāreka cāhite |  
premāẏa vihvala āi nāre sthira haite ||1832||  

śrīśacīdevīra yaiche premera vikāra |  
kahite nā jāni yaiche bhojana dom̐hāra ||1833||  

bhojana kariẏā dom̐he basilā ethāẏa |  
sthāna pariskāra mui karila tvarāẏa ||1834||  

pātra avaśeṣe harṣe laïlu sakala |  
se saba bhāvite hiẏā haïche vikala ||1835||  

nityānande laiẏā gauracandra gaṇasane |  
ethā hailā parama vihvala saṅkīrtane ||1836||  

ethā viśvambhara āpanāre prakāśaẏa |  
matsa, kūrma, varāha, vāmana ādi haẏa ||1837||  

yakhana ye bhāve prabhu āpanā prakāśe |  
takhana tā dekhe mātra prabhupriẏa dāse ||1838||  

śivera gāẏaka eka āsiẏā ethāẏa |  
gāẏa śiva-gīta, nāce, ḍamaru vājāẏa ||1839||  

maheśera bhāve prabhu dhairya nāi bāndhe |  
mui se maheśa bali carh̤‌e tāra kāndhe ||1840||  

gīte yathā—mālavastrī—  

āju śaṅkaracarita śuni  
śacītanaẏa śaṅkara bhela |  
rajata-giri jiti,		jyoti ḍagamaga,  
jagata-dhṛti hari nela ||1841||  

bhasama-bhūṣita,		aṅga-bhaṅgima,  
anaṅga-madabharahāri |  
rucira kara gahi,		śṛṅga vāẏata,  
ḍamaru-raba rucikārī ||1842||  

lola lalita,		trilocanāñcala,  
lasata vaẏana maẏaṅka |  
gaṇḍa-maṇḍala,	vimala mṛdutara,  
bhāla bhuruyuga baṅka ||1843||  

vipula pallaga,		bhūṣaṇāmbara,  
carama parama ujora |  
śirasi mañju,		jaṭāla paṭabhara,  
pekhi narahari bhora ||1844||  

maheśa-āveśa prabhu samvaraṇa kailā |  
se bhāgyavantera skandha haïte nāmilā ||1845||  

aiche bhikṣā dilā tāre prabhu daẏāmaẏa |  
puna āra bhikṣā yena karite nā haẏa ||1846||  

ethā prabhu ānande laïẏā priẏagaṇa |  
karila nirbandha rātriyoge saṅkīrtana ||1847||  

kabhu kuna sthāne kare kīrtana-vihāra |  
saṅge pāriṣada yata lekhā nāi tāra ||1848||  

tathāhi śrīcaitanyabhāgavate—  
śrīvāsa-mandire prati niśāẏa kīrtana |  
kuna dina haẏa candraśekhara-bhavana ||1849||  

nityānanda, gadādhara, advaita, śrīvāsa |  
vidyānidhi, mūrāri, hiraṇya, haridāsa ||1850||  

gaṅgādāsa, vanamālī, vijaẏa, nandana |  
jagadānanda, buddhimanta khān, nārāẏaṇa ||1851||  

kāśīśvara, vāsudeva, rāma garur̤āi |  
govinda, govindānanda sakala tathāi ||1852||  

gopīnātha, jagadīśa, śrīmāna, śrīdhara |  
sadāśiva, vākreśvara, bhūgarbha, śuklāmbhara ||1853||  

brahmānanda, puruṣodttama-sañjaẏādi yata |  
ananta caitanyabhṛtya nāma niva kata ||1854||  

se-saba sahita ekadina e aṅgane |  
divā-niśi vihvala laïẏā saṅkīrtane ||1855||  

devera durlabha nṛtya kare gaurahari |  
se suveśa-śobhā sabe dekhe netra bhari ||1856||  

gīte yathā—śrīrāga—  

campaka-kusūma,		kanaka nava kuṅkuma,  
tar̤itapuñja jini varaṇa ujora |  
jhalamala manamatha,	phānda cāndamukha,  
madhurima adhare hāsa ati thora ||1857||  

jaẏa jaẏa gaura,		naṭana janarañjana,  
bali kalikāla-garava bhara bhañjana || dhru ||1858||  

mañju, pulakakula,	balita kalevara,  
garagara nirata tarala, nahu thira |  
gada gada bhāṣa,		avaśa niśi-vāsara |  
jhara jhara kañja naẏane jhara nīra ||1859||  

nirupama cāru		caritra karuṇāmaẏa,  
patitabandhu yaśa bviśada vithāra |  
bhaṇa ghanaśyāma,	bhāga bhuẏaśaḥ rasa,  
bvitaraṇa lāgi lalita avatāra ||1860||  

punaḥ—karṇāṭa—  

nācata bhuvana-manamohana,  
campaka kanaka kañja jini varaṇā |  
subalani tanu mṛdu,		malaẏaja rañjita,  
pahiraṇa cīna vasana ghana kiraṇā ||1861||  

himakara-nikara		nindi madhurānana,  
hāsata madhura sudhā yanu jharaī |  
bhuruyuga bhṛṅga-	pām̐ti lasa locana,  
bhagamaga aruṇa kiraṇa bhara haraï ||1862||  

dolata maṇimaẏa-		hāra harata dhṛti,  
ṭalamala kuṇḍala jhalakata śravaṇe |  
cām̐cara cikura,		bhaṅgibhāra-bhare,  
vilulita hālata, timira tāra yanu pavane ||1863||  

abhinaẏa lalita,		kalita kara kiśalaẏe,  
kata śata tāla dharata paga dharaṇe |  
narahari parama		ulasa yaśa gāẏata,  
śobhā vipula kaunaka vivaraṇe ||1864||  

puna—somarāga—  

nācata gaura puruva rase bhora |  
kanaka dharādhara-		garava vibhañjana,  
jhalakata aṅga atanu-cita-cora | | dhrru ||1865||  

hāsata mṛdu mṛdu,	vadanacānda chavi,  
nāśata ghora kuluṣa ām̐dhaẏāra |  
dharaïte tāla,		tarala padapaṅkaja,  
kampaï dharaṇī sahaï nāhi bhāra ||1866||  

taruṇa aruṇa yuga,	locana bhagamaga,  
avirala vipula, pūlakakula sāji |  
garajata saghana,		siṁha jini vikrama  
bali kalikāla vipula bhaẏe bhāji ||1867||  

bhedata gagana,		gāne priẏa parikara,  
vāẏata khola lalita karatāla |  
mātala ākhila		loka bhaṇa narahari,  
bhuvana bharala yaśa viśada viśāla ||1868||  

punaḥ—āsrapañcaka—  

nirupama hemajyoti jiti varaṇā |  
saṅgīta-raṅgita raṅgita caraṇā ||1869||  

nācata gauracandra guṇamaṇiẏā |  
caudige hari hari dhani dhani dhaniẏā || dhru ||1870||  

śaradacandra jini sundara vaẏanā |  
ahaniśi premanijhare jharu naẏanā ||1871||  

vipula pulaka-paripūrita dehā |  
nija-rase bhāsi nā pāẏata thehā ||1872||  

jaga bhari pūrala e hena ānandā |  
mahimāhā vañcita dāsa govindā ||1873||  

ohe śrīnivāsa, prabhu āpana-bhavane |  
ye bhāva prakāśe tā varṇiba kuna jane ||1874||  

āi mahāvihvala haïẏā eikhāne |  
netrajale sikta haïlena saṅkīrtane ||1875||  

priẏagaṇa-saha prabhu bāhya prakāśiẏā |  
śrīvāsa-ālaẏe gelā ei patha diẏā ||1876||  

saṅkīrtanāveśe rahi śrīvāsa-bhavane |  
ethā āsi baise prabhu rajanī-vihāne ||1877||  

parama adbhuta śobhā dekhi netra bhari |  
ye ājñā karila tā karilu śīghra kari ||1878||  

ke bujhite pāre gaura-caritra gabhīra |  
saṅkīrtana vinā tilārdheka nahe thira ||1879||  

aparāhna-kāle prabhu saṅkīrtana-raṅge |  
ei pathe gaṅgātīre gelā gaṇa-saṅge ||1880||  

gaṅgātīre saṅkīrtanānande magna haiẏā |  
gaṇa-saha āilā gṛhe ei patha diẏā ||1881||  

ye bhāva-āveśe saṅkīrtana eikhāne |  
tāhā dekhilena ethā rahi bhāgyavāne ||1882||  

śrīgauracandrera śobhā bhuvanamohana |  
parama adbhuta raṅge karaẏe nartana ||1883||  

gīte yathā—dhānaśī—  

bhāla raṅge nāce mora śacīra dulāla |  
saba aṅge candana, dolaẏe vanamāla ||1884||  

viśāla hṛdaẏe gajamukutāra hāra |  
padatale tāla uṭhe nūpura-jhaṅkāra ||1885||  

chanda-vichande kata jāne aṅgabhaṅgi |  
nadīẏānagare nāi eta bar̤a raṅgī ||1886||  

kinnara karaẏe śikṣā śuni mṛdu gāna |  
gandharva tāṇḍava heri dharaẏe dhiẏāna ||1887||  

paṅkajā saṅkoca pāẏa dekhiẏā naẏane |  
hāsite vijuri-chaṭā par̤aẏe daśane ||1888||  

bām̐dhuli jiniẏā rāṅā oṭakhāni hāsa |  
o-rūpa heriẏā kānde balarāmadāsa ||1889||  

ohe śrīnivāsa, prabhu kīrtana-āveśe |  
kahite nā jāni kichu ye-bhāva prakāśe ||1890||  

ekadina ki ānanda upajila mane |  
ei pathe gelā ekā śrīvāsa-bhavane ||1891||  

sāta-prahariẏā-bhāve vilasi tathāẏa |  
ei pathe āilā nijālaẏe gaurarāẏa ||1892||  

ei puṣpavāṭī-madhye priẏagaṇa-sane |  
haïlā vihvala kṛṣṇakathā-ālāpane ||1893||  

ki baliba śrīnivāsa dekhilu ye sukha |  
se saba bhāvite ebe vidariche buka ||1894||  

ekadina ei ghare prabhu viśvambhara |  
apūrva āsane baise ullāsa antara ||1895||  

nija prāṇanātha-pāśe devī viṣṇupriẏā |  
tāmbūla yogāna, prabhu khāẏena hāsiẏā ||1896||  

henaï samaẏe nityānanda bhāvāveśe |  
calite ḍhalite āilā prabhura āvāse ||1897||  

dekhi preme vihvala nitāi digambara |  
tām̐re vastra āpane parāna viśvambhara ||1898||  

dekhi e caritra āi hāse mane mane |  
nityānande viśvarūpa-putrasama jāne ||1899||  

nityānande dila cāri sandeśa khāite |  
khāila sandeśa mahā-kautuka tāhāte ||1900||  

nityānanda-bhārāveśa bujhane nā yāẏa |  
prabhu-saha kata kathā rahiẏā ethāẏa ||1901||  

śrīnityānandera śrīkaupīna ekakhāni |  
cāhiẏā nilena gauracandra guṇamaṇi ||1902||  

se kaupīna khaṇḍa khaṇḍa kari gaurarāẏa |  
dilena sabhāre, sabhe dharila māthāẏa ||1903||  

śrīgaurasundara preme vihvala haïẏā |  
nityānanda-pādodaka sabhe khāoẏāilā ||1904||  

kaupīna-dhāraṇa āra pādodaka-pāne |  
ye premavihvala tā kahite kebā jāne ||1905||  

saṅkīrtana-sukhera samudra uthalila |  
gaṇasaha prabhu nṛtye vihvala haïla ||1906||  

gīte yathā—deśapāla—  

nṛtyata gauracandra janarañjana, nityānanda vipadabhaẏa-bhañjana,  
kañjanaẏana jiti nava nava khañjana, cāhani manamatha-parava hare |  
jhalakata dum̐hu tanu, kanaka dharādhara, naṭana ghaṭana paga, dharata dharaṇīpara, hāsa milita mukha lasata sudhākara, ucari vacana anu amiẏa jhare ||1907||  

śobhā nirupama, bhanatana āẏata, veṣṭitaparikaragaṇa guṇagaṇagāẏata,  
madhura madhura mṛdu mardana vāẏata, dhādhā dhigi dhigi dhikaṭa dhilaṅga |  
gaṇasaha suragaṇa gagana-panthagata, ghana ghana sarasa, kusumavara varayata, jaẏa jaẏa jaẏa dhvani bhuvana viẏāpata, narahari kahaba ki premataraṅga ||1908||  

punaḥ—kāmoda—  

āju ki ānanda saṅkīrtane |  
nāce gaura-nityānanda,		parama ānanda-kanda  
priẏa pariṣadavṛnda sane ||1909||  

nāce bole bhāla bhāla,		bāje khola karatāla,  
sabhe mahā vihvala premāẏa |  
nadīra pravāha pārā,		sabhāra naẏane dhārā,  
keha keha par̤e kāru gāẏa ||1910||  


keha vā pulakabhare,		huṅkāra garjana kare,  
kām̐pe keha thira haite nāre |  
keho kāru pāne cāẏā,		dui bāhu pasāriẏā,  
kole kari chār̤ite nā pāre ||1911||  

keha kāru pāẏa dhare,		padadhūli laẏa śire,  
keha bhūme gar̤āgar̤i yāẏa |  
prabhu-bhṛtya eka rīti,		dekhi narahari ati,  
ānande prabhura guṇa gāẏa ||1912||  

yakhana ye prabhura āveśa bhakta-mele |  
takhana serūpa krīr̤ā kare kutūhale ||1913||  

mahāprabhu nityānanda-haridāsa prati śrīkṛṣṇabhajana-pracāre ājñā—  

ekadina prabhu ekā vasi divyāsane |  
sakaruṇa-netre nirikhaẏe cāripāne ||1914||  

priẏa nityānanda haridāse kahe yāha |  
‘śrīkṛṣṇa bhajite ājñā sarvatra yānāha’ ||1915||  

prabhu-ājñā laiẏā dom̐he gelā ei pathe |  
dom̐hāra ānanda yata ke pāre kahite ||1916||  

sarvatra kahiẏā tā prabhure jānāilā |  
sabhāsaha prabhudāsye uddhāriẏā nilā ||1917||  

prabhura jagāi mādhāi-uddhāra—  

svagaṇe veṣṭita prabhu basilā ethāi |  
stuti kaila dasyu dui—jagāi-mādhāi ||1918||  

jagāi-mādhāi dui jane dekhibāre |  
viṣṇupriẏā saha āi baise ei ghare ||1919||  

kahe śrīnivāsa, gauracandra eikhāne |  
sabhāsaha vihvala nācaẏe saṅkīrtane ||1920||  

gīte yathā—dhānaśī—  

nāce śacīra dulāla raṅge |  
advaita nitāi, gadādhara		śrīvāsādi parikara saṅge ||1921||  
aṅgabhaṅgi ki madhura chām̐de |  
padabhare mahī,			kare ṭalamala,  
ke tāhe dhairaya bāndhe ||1922||  

nānā tāle diẏā karatāli |  
govinda mādhava,		vasu yaśa gāẏa,  
caudige śobhaẏe bhāli ||1923||  

gorācām̐da mukhe haribole |  
jagāi-mādhāi,		dohe heri bāhu  
pasāri karaẏe kole ||1924||  

gorācāndera paraśa pāẏā |  
jagāi-mādhāi,		nāce bhuja tuli  
bhāvete vihvala haiẏā ||1925||  

dohe loṭāya dharaṇītale |  
kām̐pe tanu anu-		pama pulakita,  
titaẏe ākhera jale ||1926||  

gorā-karuṇā-prakāśa dekhi |  
nāce suragaṇa		gaganete rahi,  
saghane jur̤āẏa ām̐khi ||1927||  

ke nā dhāẏa se karuṇā-āśe |  
jaẏa jaẏa dhvani		avani bharala,  
bhaṇe ghanaśyāma dāse ||1928||  

prabhu nṛtya dekhi sabe hailā vimohita |  
vadhū-saha āi dekhi hailā ullasita ||1929||  

kṛṣṇapremavihvala mahāprabhura vibhinna līlā—  

saṅkīrtanāveśe prabhu laiẏ̈ā parikare |  
gaṅgāẏa kariẏā jala-krīr̤ā āilā ghare ||1930||  

caraṇa pākhāli tulasīre praṇamiẏā |  
bhuñje viṣṇu-prasādānna e ghare basiẏā ||1931||  

bhakṣaṇādi sāri ethā karilā śaẏana |  
alakṣita āsiẏā sevila devagaṇa ||1932||  

prabhura e līlā vā bujhiba kona jane |  
dekhilu ye saba tā sadāi jāge mane ||1933||  

ekadina prabhu śrīvāsera bār̤ī gelā |  
tām̐ra śāśur̤īre kṛpā kari ghare āilā ||1934||  

ekadina prabhu ei pathe gaṇasane |  
saṅkīrtanāveśe cāle nagara-bhramaṇe ||1935||  

nagara bhramiẏā prabhu ullāsa hiẏāẏa |  
gaṇasaha gṛhe āsi baisaẏe ethāẏa ||1936||  

ke bujhe caritra, prabhu kahe sarvajane |  
premaśūnya dehatyāga kariba ekhāne ||1937||  

ihā bali gaṅgāẏa par̤āẏe jhām̐pa diẏā |  
nityānanda-haridāsa ānaẏe tuliẏā ||1938||  

ithe ye kautuka tāhā ke kahite pāre |  
saṅkīrtana sukhe prabhu sadāi vihare ||1939||  

ei dekha, bār̤īra nikaṭa ramya sthāne |  
haïlena parama vihvala saṅkīrtane ||1940||  

gīte yathā—baṅgāla—  

nācata gauracahndra guṇadhāma |  
jhalakata aṅga-		kirāṇe mana rañjana,  
kanaka meru dūre dāminī-dāma || dhru ||1941||  

bandhura vadana,		madana-mada-maradana,  
madhurima-hāsa yuvati-dhṛtihāri |  
śrutijiti taruṇa, 		aruṇa maṇikuṇḍala,  
ṭalamala naẏanayugala chabi bhāri ||1942||  

cām̐cara cikana,		ke kusumāñcita,  
capala cāru ure maṇḍita māla |  
abhinava bāhu,		bhaṅgibhara nirupama,  
dharata caraṇatale sulalita tāla ||1943||  

pam̐hu calu pāśa,		lasata priẏaparikara,  
gāẏata madhura rāga rasa māti |  
ulasita sakala,		bhuvana bhaṇa narahari,  
vāẏata khola khamaka bahu bhām̐ti ||1944||  

punarvelāvalī—  

nācata gauracandra naṭabhūpa |  
manamatha lākha,		garava bhara bhañjana,  
akhila bhuvana-janarañjana rūpa || dhru ||1945||  

avirata atula,		bhāvabhare garagara,  
garajata ati adbhuta rucikārī |  
maṅgalamaẏapada,	dharata dharaṇī para,  
karata bhaṅgi bhujayugala pasāri ||1946||  

hāsata madhura,		adhara mṛdu lāvaṇi,  
śarada-cānda jini vadana vilāsa |  
ṭalamala aruṇa,		kamaladala locana,  
kaune karaẏa kata rasa parakāśa ||1947||  

gāẏata madhura,		bhaktagaṇa nava nava,  
kinnara-nikara darapa karu cūra |  
uthalala prema-		sindhu mahī bhāsala,  
narahari kumati paraśa rahu dūra ||1948||  

candraśekharācāryagṛhe mahāprabhura lakṣmīveśe nṛtya—  

saṅkīrtanāveśe ethā śacīra tanaẏa |  
sadāśiva buddhimanta khām̐ne ḍāki kaẏa ||1949||  

āji candraśekharācāryera gṛhe giẏā |  
lakṣmī ādi veśete nāciba sabe laiẏā ||1950||  

śaṅkha, śār̤ī, kām̐culī, svarṇādi alaṅkāra |  
yogya yogya veśa sajja karaha sabhāra ||1951||  

eta kahi gauracandra priẏagaṇa sane |  
ei pathe gelā candraśekhara-bhavane ||1952||  

tathā nānā veśe nṛtya kari viśvambhara |  
ethā āsi basilā veṣṭita parikara ||1953||  

śrīgauracandrera raṅga ke bujhite pāre |  
bhaktasaṅge viharaẏe vividha prakāre ||1954||  

advaitāryera prabhu kṛpāprāpti āśāẏa jñāna-yogā-vyākhyā—  

advaitere gurubhakti kare gaurarāẏa |  
tāhāte advaitācārya mahāduḥkha pāẏa ||1955||  

advaitera mane haila aiche kārya kari |  
yāte mora śāsti prabhu kare cule dhāri ||1956||  

eta vicāriẏā haridāse laiẏā saṅge |  
kona chale vidāẏa haïẏā cale raṅge ||1957||  

prabhu-krodha janmāite upāẏa sṛjila |  
‘bhakti chār̤i jñāna śreṣṭha’ vyākhyā ārambhila ||1958||  

nija gṛhe vasi dibvya pīr̤āra upare |  
mahādarpe ‘jñāna śreṣṭha’ bujhāẏa sabāre ||1959||  

advaitācāryera vyākhyā śuniẏā sakale |  
paraspara kahe kata rahiẏā virale ||1960||  

sītādevī śrīṭhākurāṇīra prati kaẏa |  
nā bujhiẏā evā kona raṅga prakāśaẏa ||1961||  

avaśya haïba ethā prabhura gamana |  
eta kahi karaẏe sāmagrī āẏojana ||1962||  

sakala jānaẏe antaryāmī gauracandra |  
eikhāne basiẏā hāsaẏe manda manda ||1963||  

advaitasaṅkalpasiddhi karibāra tare |  
nagarabhramaṇa-chale cale śāntipure ||1964||  

saṅge nityānanda, gati adbhuta dom̐hāra |  
dekhi se mādhuryā dhairya dhare śakti kāra ||1965||  

lalitapurete kṛpā kari sannyāsīre |  
gaṅgāpathe dom̐he śīghra gelā śāntipure ||1966||  

advaita ācārya prabhu gamana jāniẏā |  
‘jñāna śreṣṭha’ bākhāne adhika matta haiẏā ||1967||  

advaita-ālaẏe prabhu karilā gamana |  
acyutānandādi vande prabhura caraṇa ||1968||  

sabā prati śubhadṛṣṭi kari goracandra |  
advaita sammukhe gelā saṅge nityānanda ||1969||  

prabhu krodhe advaita ācārye jijñāsaẏa |  
‘jñāna, bhakti haite śreṣṭha kaha kebā haẏa ?’ ||1970||  

‘sarvaśreṣṭha jñāna haẏa’ advaita kahilā |  
śuni mahākrodhe prabhu bāhya pāsarilā ||1971||  

mahābalavān prabhu śrīgaurasundara |  
lāpha diẏā uṭhe śīghra pīr̤āra upara ||1972||  

advaitera cule dhari pār̤e uṭhānete |  
advaite kilāẏa sukomala dui hāte ||1973||  

sarvatattva-jñātā sītā jagata-jananī |  
vyagratā karaẏe kata kahe mṛdu vāṇī ||1974||  

haridāsa trāsete rahaẏe ekapāśe |  
nityānanda raṅge ati manda manda hāse ||1975||  

prabhu krodhe garjiẏā īśvarya prakāśila |  
śāsti pāi advaitera ānanda bārh̤‌ila ||1976||  

hāte tāli diẏā nāce śrīadvaita rāẏa |  
prabhura caraṇa-dhūli karaẏe māthāẏa ||1977||  

advaita kahila kata—śuni gaurahari |  
karaẏe krandana advaitere kole kari ||1978||  

nityānanda-haridāsa karaẏe krandana |  
kāndaẏe advaita sītā ādi priẏagaṇa ||1979||  

advaita-tanaẏa śrīacyutānanda kānde |  
advaita-bhavane keho thira nāhi bāndhe ||1980||  

advaita karilā stuti, prabhu vara dila |  
mahā jaẏa jaẏa-dhvani bhuvana bharila ||1981||  

advaitera gṛhe haila prabhura bhojana |  
char̤āilā anna padmābvatīra nandana ||1982||  

kichudina rahi prabhu advaita-bhavane |  
navadvīpe āse mahā ullasita mane ||1983||  

jñānayoga prasaṅge kahiẏe kichu āra |  
advaita antara bujhe aiche śakti kāra ||1984||  

advaitācāryera śākhā—śaṅkara nāmete |  
jñāna-pakṣe tām̐ra niṣṭhā haila bhālamate ||1985||  

advaita śaṅkara prati kahe vāre vāre |  
‘manorathasiddhi mui kailu e prakāre ||1986||  

chār̤a chār̤a ore re pāgala ! naṣṭa hailā’ |  
tem̐ho nā chār̤e tāre advaita tyāga kailā ||1987||  

mahābahirmukha bīja karila ropaṇa |  
krame vṛddhi haïba jānila vijñagaṇa ||1988||  

nityānandādvaita, haridāsa prabhusaṅge |  
śāntipura haite nadīẏāẏa āilā raṅge ||1989||  

nija gṛhe āsi, prabhu basilā ethāẏa |  
prabhuke dekhite loka caturdike dhāẏa ||1990||  

śrīvāsa, mukunda, vakreśvara ādi yata |  
haïlena sabe saṅkīrtane unamata ||1991||  

saṅkīrtana-sukhera samudre prabhu bhāse |  
ei patha diẏā gelā śrīvāsa-āvāse ||1992||  

śrīvāsera ghare sukha prakāśi āsiẏā |  
murārira ghare gelā ei patha diẏā ||1993||  

tathā haite āsi ethā baise viśvambhara |  
caturdike śobhaẏe sakala parikara ||1994||  

śacīdevīra advaitapadadhūli grahaṇa dvārā vaiṣṇavāparādha-socana-śikṣā—  

adbhuta bhaṅgite prabhu kahe priẏagaṇe |  
aparādha kailā mātā advaitera sthāne ||1995||  

‘yadi tām̐ra padadhūli dharena māthāẏa |  
tabe tām̐ra sthāne tām̐ra aparādha yāẏa’ ||1996|  

etta kahi bhaktiyoga karaẏe prakāśa |  
āira ye aparādha śuna śrīnivāsa ||1997||  

‘viśvarūpa baise sadā advaita-sabhāẏa |  
karilā sannyāsa tem̐ho āpana icchāẏa ||1998||  

putrera vicchede āi vyākula haïẏā |  
mane vicāraẏe ethā kāndiẏā kāndiẏā ||1999||  

advaita gosāñira daẏa mātra nāi cite |  
viśvarūpe bāhira karila ghara haite ||2000||  

e pūtreo sthira haite nā dena ācāryā |  
mahāvijña haïẏā kena hena kārya ||2001||  

ācārya gosāñi mora dui putra nila’ |  
eta mane karitei bhaẏa upajila ||2002||  

ei aparādha mātra karilena āi |  
ihā śuni advaita āilā ei ṭhām̐i ||2003||  

śrīśacīmāẏera kahi mahimā apāra |  
haïlā mūrcchita preme kubera-kumāra ||2004||  

samaẏa bujhiẏā āi ethāẏa āilā |  
advaita-caraṇa-dhūli mastake dharilā ||2005||  

haïlena harṣa gauracandra bhagavān |  
jananīra lakṣmye anye kaila sāvadhāna ||2006||  

premabhaktiratna dātā śacīra tanaẏa |  
nirantara saṅkīrtanānande vilasaẏa ||2007||  

saṅkīrtanāveśe prabhu āpanā nā jāne |  
ei pathe calilena nagara-bhramaṇe ||2008||  

nagara-bhramaṇe mahāraṅga prakāśiẏā |  
gaṇasaha ethā prabhu baise harṣa haiẏā ||2009||  

vrajera vilāsa sadā uthale hiẏāẏa |  
sumadhurasvare mukundādi tāhā gāẏa ||2010||  

nijaśuṇa śunite prabhura bar̤a sādha |  
ke bujhite pāre cāru carita agādha ||2011||  

prabhura iṅgite gadādhara eikhāne |  
racaẏe prabhura veśa puṣpera bhūṣaṇe ||2012||  

dāsa gadādhara prabhupriẏa narahari |  
veśera sāmagrī saba dena sajja kari ||2013||  

bhuvanamohana veśa racila prabhura |  
ye vāreka dekhe tām̐ra dhairya yāẏa dūra ||2014||  

veśera suṣamā ye upamā nāi tāẏa |  
muruchaẏe kāmakoṭi aṅgera chaṭāẏa ||2015||  

prabhupriẏagaṇa cāhi cāndamukha-pāne |  
yerūpa haïla tā kahite kebā jāne ||2016||  

āpani nichaẏe bhāva āveśa sabāra |  
kare ārātrika, sukha śobhā nāi pāra ||2017||  

gīte yathā—gaurī—  

jaẏa jaẏa ārati gaurakiśora |  
lasata siṁhāsane		janu kanakācala,  
ḍagamaga jagata-yuvatī-cita-cora | | dhru ||2018||  

śrīadvaita premabhare,		garagara ārati,  
karu nija nāthe nehāri |  
maṇigaṇa jaṭita su-		kanaka thāri para,  
damakata dīpa durita tamahāri ||2019||  

dakṣiṇa bhāge,		bhāti rīti adbhuta,  
nityānandacandra rasabhora |  
vāme gadādhara,		sarasa bhaṅgi tahi  
kou dharata nalva chatra ujora ||2020||  

śrīnivāsa vara-		yata kusumāvalī,  
cāmara karu narahaṇi anivāra |  
śuklāmbara vara,		caracata candana,  
guptamurāri karata jaẏakāra ||2021||  

mādhava, vāsu-		ghoṣa , puruṣottama  
vijaẏa, mukunda ādi guṇi-bhūpa |  
gāẏata madhura,		rāga śruti mūruchana,  
grāma sapta svara bheda anupa ||2022||  

bājata muraja,		mṛdaṅga caṅgar̤‌aka,  
vīṇa, viṣāṇa, veṇu calu ora |  
ghana ghana ghaṇṭa,	jhamakata jhām̐jharī,  
jhana na na jhām̐ja garaje ghana ghora ||2023||  

nācata parama-		haraṣa vakreśvara,  
sarasa bhām̐ti gati nāṭaka suḍhāra |  
ughaṭata dhikaṭa,		dhikaṭa dhidhi kaṭa,  
taka thai thai thai ti vividha parakāra ||2024||  

vivaśa purura rase,	rasika gadādhara,  
śrīdhara, gaurīdāsa, haridāsa |  
ke viracaba saba,		bhakata matta ati,  
nirakhi gauramukha-madhurima hāsa ||2025||  

suragaṇa gagane,		magana gaṇasaha,  
surapati kata yatane karata parihāra |  
pārvatīpati catu-		rānana pulakita  
jhara jhara naẏane jharata jaladhāra ||2026||  

tribhuvana ulasa,		śeṣa yaśa varaṇata,  
stuti karu muni nava nāma ucāri |  
narahari pahu vraja-		bhūṣaṇa rasamaẏa,  
nadīẏāpura paramānandakārī ||2027||  

parama maṅgala ārātrika sandarśane |  
haila sabe vihvala āpanā nāhi jāne ||2028||  

nānā bhakṣa dravya laiẏā prabhure bhuñjāẏa |  
bhuñjaẏe kautuka sabe prabhura ājñāẏa ||2029||  

haïla aneka rātri dekhi sarvajana |  
nija nija sthāne sabe karilā śaẏana ||2030||  

śuibena gauracandra jāni gadādhara |  
racilena śayyā sukomala manohara ||2031||  

śuite calena prabhu haiẏā ullasita |  
gādāi-racita mālya-candane bhūṣita ||2032||  

ei ghare śaẏana karilā viśvambhara |  
śuilena nikaṭe paṇḍita gadādhara ||2033||  

dum̐hu vākyāmṛta-pāne dom̐he magna hailā |  
ke bujhite pāre gaura-gadādhara-līlā ||2034||  

prabhāte jāgiẏā gadādhara harṣamane |  
karaẏe ye kārya tā varṇaẏe vijñagaṇe ||2035||  

tathāhi śrīcaitanyacarite dvitīẏa prakrame—  
gadādharo mahāprājño brāhmaṇaḥ satkulodbhavaḥ |  
premabhaktaśca tatpādasannikarṣe’bhitiṣṭhati ||2036||  

tena sārddhaṁ rajanyāṁ sa tiṣṭhannūce śubhākṣaram |  
dātavyaṁ bhavatā prātarvaiṣṇavebhyaḥ prasādakam ||2037||  

ityuktvā gātramālyāni dadau tasya kare hariḥ |  
tataḥ prabhāte vimale te sarve samupāgatāḥ ||2038||  

yasmai yasmai ca yaddattaṁ tattasmai sampradattavān |  
tataste hṛṣṭamanasaḥ snātvā suranadījale ||2039||  

pūjaẏitvā jagannathaṁ naivedyaṁ viniyujya ca |  
punastaṁ devadeveśamājagmurmuditāśaẏaḥ ||2040||  

gadādhara pratyehaṁ taṁ candanenānulepanam |  
kṛtvā mālyādi gātreṣu dadāti satataṁ mudā ||2041||  

śaẏanīẏe gṛhe śayyāṁ kṛtvā tatsannidhau sukham |  
svapiti śraddhaẏā yuktaḥ śṛṇvaṁsyāmṛtaṁ vacaḥ ||2042||  

sa tu gadādharapaṇḍitaḥ sattamaḥ  
satatamasya samīpasusaṅgataḥ |  
anudilaṁ bhajate nijajīvita  
priẏatamaṁ tamatispṛhaẏā yutaḥ ||2043||  

niśi tadīẏasamīpagataḥ sthiraḥ  
śaẏanamutsuka eva karoti saḥ |  
viharaṇāmtamasya nirantaraṁ  
tadupabhuktamanena nirantaram ||2044||  

ohe śrīnivāsa prabhu rajanī-vihāne |  
vilase paramānande bhaktagoṣṭhī-sane ||2045||  

ethā divyāsane baise prabhu gaurarāẏa |  
karite darśana ngariẏā loka dhāẏa ||2046||  

śrīmanmahāprabhura bhaktavṛndera prati karuṇā prakāśa o nirbandhasahakāre śrīharināmopadeśa pradāna—  

prabhu-pāśe āsi praṇamaẏe vāravāra |  
prabhu kahe—‘kṛṣṇa bhakti haüka sabhāra’ ||2047||  

sabhā prati kari prabhu karuṇā aśeṣa |  
harināma mahāmantra kare upadeśa ||2048||  

‘hare kṛṣṇa hare kṛṣṇa kṛṣṇa kṛṣṇa hare hare |  
hare rāma hare rāma rāma rāma hare hare’ ||2049||  

punaḥ prabhu kahe bhāi nirbandha kariẏā |  
‘harināma japa sabhe kara ghare giẏā ||2050||  

haïba sakala siddhi mantrera pratāpe |  
pāibā paramānanda ei mantrajape’ ||2051||  

punaḥ danta tṛṇa dhari kahe sabā prati |  
‘karite śrīkṛṣṇa kīrtana divārāti’ ||2052||  

aiche śrīmukhera upadeśa sabhe pāi |  
praṇamiẏā mantra japa kare ghare yāi ||2053||  

prabhura ājñāẏa sabe ullāsa antare |  
saṁkīrtana ārambha karilā ghare ghare ||2054||  

kādi duṣṭa kīrtana sahite nāre kabhu |  
karila kīrtana-vāda śunilena prabhu ||2055||  

śuni mahākrodhayukta haiẏā gaurahari |  
āpanāra tattva prakāśaye darpa kari ||2056||  

ghana ghana huṅkāra karaẏe mahāraṅge |  
nagarakīrtane prabhu sāje gaṇasaṅge ||2057||  

haïla sarvatra dhvani—‘śacīra nandana |  
nagare nagare āji kariba kīrtana’ ||2058||  

nagariẏā loke ājñā kaila gaurarāẏa |  
‘godhūli-samaẏe sabe āsibe ethāẏa’ ||2059||  

nagariẏā loka mahāpraphulla hṛdaẏa |  
sājiẏā āilā ethā śobhā atiśaẏa ||2060||  

lokera nāhika anta ohe śrīnivāsa |  
jaẏa jaẏa śabda vyāpi e bhūmi ākāśa ||2061||  

śrīgaurasundara mahā ullasita-mane |  
āge saṅkīrtanārambha kaila eikhāne ||2062||  

bhuvanamohana-veśe nāce gauracandra |  
vāme gadādhara se dakṣiṇe nityānanda ||2063||  

advaita, śrīvāsa, haridāsa, vakreśvara |  
narahari dāsa, gadādhara, dāmodara ||2064||  

murāri, mukunda, vāsu, govindādi yata |  
saba nāce gāẏa śobhā ke kahila kata ||2065||  

ethā mahāvihvala haïẏā saṅkīrtane |  
karilā sampradābaddha gaurāṅga āpane ||2066||  

prabhura ādeśe harṣa śrīadvaitarāẏa |  
ethā haite cale āge eka sampradāẏa ||2067||  

tām̐ra nṛtya gīte keu sthira nāhi bāndhe |  
kibā strī-bālaka sabe phukāriẏā kānde ||2068||  

ethā haite pṛthaka pṛthaka sampradāẏa |  
śrīvāsādi cale mahāraṅge nāce gāẏa ||2069||  

eka sampradāẏa prabhu śarīra nandana |  
ei pathe cale śobhā bhuvana mohana ||2070||  

eikhāne āi putravadhura sahite |  
premāẏa vihvala hailā se śobhā dekhite ||2071||  

prakāśe adbhuta līlā prabhu gaurarāẏa |  
sabe saṁkīrtanānanda-samudre ḍubāẏa ||2072||  

eka mukhe ki baliba se adbhuta kathā |  
nagara-kīrtana kari prabhu āila ethā ||2073||  

eikhāne baisaẏe veṣṭita sarvajane |  
haila niśi bhora kṛṣṇa-caritra kathane ||2074||  

ekadina gauracandra nadīẏā nagare |  
calaẏe bhramaṇe vaiṣṇavera ghare ghare ||2075||  

prathamei ei pathe karilā gamana |  
caturdike veṣṭita parama priẏagaṇa ||2076||  

sarvatra bhramaṇa prabhu kari mahāraṅge |  
gṛhe āsi ethāi baisaẏe gaṇa saṅge ||2077||  

ohe śrīnivāsa ekadina eikhāne |  
bhuvanamohana-veśe nāce saṅkīrtane ||2078||  

prabhura caritra kebā bujhibāre pāre |  
saṅkīrtane anugraha kare yāre tāre ||2079||  

putra saha baṅgadeśī vipra śuddhācāra |  
bhikṣuka brāhmaṇa, vanamālī nāma tāra ||2080||  

tem̐ho gauracandre dekhe śyāmala sundara |  
śire śikhipuccha, paridheẏa pītāmbara ||2081||  

adhare sparśaẏe vaṁśī dekhiẏā vihvala |  
‘ei kṛṣṇa kṛṣṇa’ bali kare kolāhala ||2082||  

ki baliba vanamālī-vipra bhāgyavāne |  
dilena amūlya premaratna eikhāne ||2083||  

ethā prabhu bhakte nāma-mahimā kahila |  
par̤uẏā adhama arthavāde duḥkha dila ||2084||  

gaṇasaha sacela karilā gaṅgāsnāna |  
duliẏāo kabhu nā dekhila mukha tāna ||2085||  

ekadina saṅkīrtanānande gaurarāẏa |  
eka āsrabīja raṅge ropila ethāẏa ||2086||  

sei kṣaṇe janmi vṛkṣa phalite lāgila |  
pār̤i pakva āsra bahu kṛṣṇe samarpila ||2087||  

nāhika valkala aṣṭi amṛta sosara |  
ekaphale pūrṇa haẏa ekera udara ||2088||  

bhuñjila se phala prabhu bhakte bhuñjāilā |  
niti vāra māsa phale, e adbhuta līlā ||2089||  

ekadina eikhāne kīrtanasamaẏa |  
haila mahā meghaghaṭā dekhi lāge bhaẏa ||2090||  

mandirā laïẏā prabhu ethā dām̐r̤āite |  
megha ur̤i gela sabe haïlā harṣa cite ||2091||  

lokaśikṣā lāgi prabhu svatantra īśvara |  
gaṇasaha mārjanā karaẏe viṣṇughara ||2092||  

tathāhi śrīkṛṣṇacaitanyacarite dvitīẏa-prakrame—  
athāparadine devo bhaktiṁ saṁśikṣaẏan svakān |  
devālaẏān yayau vipraiḥ sārddhaṁ sanmārjanīkaraḥ ||2093||  

kuddālaṁ cāṁśabhāgoṣu dhaṭīṁ kaṭivare vahan |  
netavastrakṛtoṣṇīṣo bālasūryasamaprabhaḥ ||2094||  

ācāryādyā mahātmanaḥ kuddālamārjanīkarāḥ |  
kṛṣṇasya haḍipā bhūtvā dvāraṁ devālaẏasya te ||2095||  

bhittiṁ ca mārjaẏāmāsuḥ saha kṛṣṇena sadguṇāḥ |  
evasprakāraṁ nṛhareḥ śikṣāṁ śatasahasraśaḥ |  
bhagavān svātmatantre’pi kāruṇyenābhyaśikṣaẏat ||2096||  

ekadina gopī gopī bolaẏe ethāi |  
keha kahe kṛṣṇa kena nā bole nimāi ||2097||  

nā bujhi āśaẏa sei par̤uẏā adhama |  
aiche kata kahe śuni hailā rudrasama ||2098||  

ṭheṅgā hāte dhāẏa prabhu tāhāre mārite |  
palāẏa brāhmaṇa mahā-bhaẏa pāẏa cite ||2099||  

e-par̤uẏā mili āra par̤uẏāra sane |  
nindaẏe prabhure yāẏa ye vā laẏa mane ||2100||  

prabhura nindāẏa par̤uẏāra buddhināśa |  
supaṭhita vidyā kāru nā haẏa prakāśa ||2101||  

prabhura ye mane tāhā prakāśa nā kare |  
gaṇasaha kīrtane vilase nija-ghare ||2102||  

ekadina keśavabhāratī ethā āilā |  
tām̐re namaskari nimantriẏā bhikṣā dilā ||2103||  

nā jāniẏe ki kathā haïla paraspare |  
bhāratī gelena śīghra kaṇṭakanagare ||2104||  

śrīvāsera gṛhe giẏā āsi viśvambhara |  
ethāi baisaẏe saṅge priẏa gadādhara ||2105||  

snāna kari viṣṇupūjā karibāre cale |  
mukha vakṣa vastra bhije naẏanera jale ||2106||  

netradhārā nivārite nāre gaurarāẏa |  
gadādhara viṣṇu pūje prabhura ājñāẏa ||2107||  

vrajera vilāse prabhu magna atiśaẏa |  
nirantara sei kathā gadādhara kaẏa ||2108||  

ke bujhite pāre gauracandrera vilāsa |  
karaẏe sampūrṇa sakalera abhilāṣa ||2109||  

viṣṇupriẏādevīra janmāẏa paritoṣa |  
aiche kārya kare yāte māẏera santoṣa ||2110||  

ohe śrīnivāsa, ei prabhura bhavane |  
dekhāila ye ye līlā kaila ye ye sthāne ||2111||  

e sakala sthāna-sandarśane duḥkha-kṣaẏa |  
devera durlabha premabhakti labhya haẏa ||2112||  

ebe bāṭī-bahirbhūta sthāna dekhāiba |  
yathā ye vilāsa tāhā kichu jānāiba ||2113||  

bālyakālavadhi bāṭī-bahirbhūta sthāne |  
kailā prabhu adbhuta vilāsa gaṇasane ||2114||  

se sakala sthāna sandarśana karāiẏā |  
punaḥ e bāṭīte sthāna dekhāba āsiẏā ||2115||  

sthāne ye prakāra tāhāo jānāiba |  
ekhane se saba kathā kahite nāriba ||2116||  

aiche kata kahi prabhu-bhavana haïte |  
calaẏe īśāna śrīnivāsādi-sahite ||2117||  

śrīnivāsa prati kahe madhura vacane |  
ethā bālyakāle prabhu khele śiśu-sane ||2118||  

ohe śrīnivāsa, ei kadambera tale |  
khele digambara prabhu bālakera mele ||2119||  

prabhura apūrva śobhā dekhi śiṣyagaṇa |  
prabhu ūrdhvamukhe kare vṛkṣa nirīkṣaṇa ||2120||  

kadambera phula māge yāra tām̐ra ṭhām̐i |  
sabhe kahe—‘ebe phula nā haẏa nimāi’ ||2121||  

śuni ardha kāndane adbhuta śodbhā yena |  
dui netre aśrubindu-yukta muktā yena ||2122||  

sabhā-prati kahe prabhu śrīcandravadane |  
pāibe avaśya puṣpa dekhaha esthāne ||2123||  

kona bhāgyavanta vṛkṣapāne nirākhite |  
dekhe eka puṣpa tem̐ha pār̤ila turite ||2124||  

nimāira hāte puṣpa diẏā kole kaila |  
sakalera mane mahā-vismaẏa janmila ||2125||  

ei baṭavṛkṣatale putre kole laiẏā |  
ṣaṣṭhī pūje yāi nānā upahāra diẏā ||2126||  

ethā chila eka nimba-vṛkṣa purātana |  
phalahīna puṣpera saugandha vilakṣaṇa ||2127||  

atyanta nibir̤a chāẏā śobhā atiśaẏa |  
vṛkṣopari kabhu kona pakṣī nā baisaẏa ||2128||  

yatadina gṛha rahilena viśvambhara |  
vṛkṣatale kaila krīr̤ā ati manohara ||2129||  

gaurīdāsa paṇḍitere prabhu ājñā kailā |  
tem̐ho sei vṛkṣe dui mūrti prakāśilā ||2130|  

haïlena yaiche dui prabhura prakāśa |  
ye ati adbhuta kathā adbuta vilāsa ||2131||  

gaurīdāsa paṇḍita parama premamaẏa |  
nityānanda-caitanyera priẏa atiśaẏa ||2132||  

ki baliba nimāicām̐dera krīr̤ākathā |  
āpanāra icchāẏa phiraẏe yathā tathā ||2133||  

yata upadrava kare bandhuvarga-ghare |  
se saba kahite se ananta śakti dhare ||2134||  

ei vipragṛhe ekadina viśvambhara |  
dugdha curi kari piẏe nirbhaẏa antara ||2135||  

śikāẏa dadhira bhāṇḍa dekhi bārh̤‌e sukha |  
bhāṇḍa chidra kari tāra tale pāte mukha ||2136||  

kari dadhi bhakṣaṇa calaẏe dhīre dhīre |  
vipra āsi dharila nimāira vāma kare ||2137||  

biprapade dhari prabhu kahe vāravāra |  
āra nā kariba ihā dohāi tomāra ||2138||  

śuni vipra dadhibinduyukta mukha dekhi |  
haïlā vihvala pālaṭite nāre ām̐khi ||2139||  

nimāicāndere vipra kahe vāravāra |  
pratidina dadhi-dugdha khāibe āmāra ||2140||  

aiche nānā upadrava kare ghare ghare |  
bāhye se sabhāra krodhe, ullāsa antare ||2141||  

ei pathe bhāgyavanta cora duijana |  
viśvambhare ghare rākhi kaila palāẏana ||2142||  

eikhāne dhūlā laiẏā khele gaurahari |  
tāhe ye adbhuta śobhā kahite nā pāri ||2143||  

ohe śrīnivāsa, dekha sthāna e nirjana |  
ethā chilā gupte sei tairthika brāhmaṇa ||2144||  

jagadīśa hiraṇya viprera e ālaẏa |  
yāhāra naivedya ekādaśīte bhuñjaẏa ||2145||  

ethā vasi vipragaṇa sumadhura bhāṣe |  
nimāira cāñcalyakalā kahaẏe ullāse ||2146||  

ei dekha jāhnavīra pulina sundara |  
śiśu saṅge khele ethā śacīra kumāra ||2147||  

se sakala khelā kehu nā dekhe nā śune |  
se sakala khelā khele mahāharṣa-mane ||2148||  

ei pathe murāriguptera āgamana |  
jñāna-vyākhyākāle kare hastera cālana ||2149||  

prabhu seirūpe tāre vidrūpa karaẏa |  
tām̐ra gṛhe gelā tām̐ra bhojana-samaẏa ||2150||  

mutileka tāra thāle kahi tattvajñāna |  
ei dekha murāriguptera vāsasthāna ||2151||  

gaṅgātīre dekha e apūrva devatāẏa |  
sarvasanoratha-siddhi ihāra kṛpāẏa ||2152||  

gaṅgāsnāna kari deve pūje kalyāgaṇa |  
akasmāt āilena śacīra nandana ||2153||  

kalyāgaṇa-madhye vasi kare nānā raṅga |  
se saba dekhite bārh̤‌e sukhera taraṅga ||2154||  

vallabha-duhitā ethā āilā āra dine |  
ki baliba ye kautuka haïla tām̐ra sane |||2155||  

ei pathe śiśugaṇa-saṅge viśvambhara |  
pratidina theliẏā yāẏena nija-ghara ||2156||  

ethāi kalaha kare anya śiśusane |  
se sabhāre jinaẏe nimāira saṅgigaṇe ||2157||  

cañcalera śiromaṇi nimāi sundara |  
cañcala bālakagaṇa saṅge nirantara ||2158||  

jāhnavīra ei ghāṭe śacīra kumāra |  
kare upadrava yata lekhā nāi tāra ||2159||  

brāhmaṇa-sajjana bāhye krodhayukta haïẏā |  
snānakāle se cāñcalya miśre kahe giẏā ||2160||  

bālikā sakala nimāira cañcalatā |  
kahe śacīmāye giẏā se adbhuta kathā ||2161||  

ei vṛkṣatale viśvarūpa mahāśaẏa |  
‘nimāi manuṣya nahe’ mane vicāraẏa ||2162||  

ethā śrīadvaita ādi prabhu-priẏagaṇa |  
jīvera kumati dekhi karaẏe krandana ||2163||  

viśvarūpa vyākhyā kare kṛṣṇabhakti sāra |  
śuniẏā advaitadeva karaẏe huṅkāra ||2164||  

viśvarūpe kole laïẏā advaita nācaẏa |  
ethā sarvabhaktira ānanda atiśaẏa ||2165||  

ethā vasi kṛṣṇera caritra sabhe kaẏa |  
śuni nija-kathā āilā śacīra tanaẏa ||2166||  

digambara dhūlāẏa dhusara sabhe dekhi |  
haïlā mugdha keha phirāite nāre ām̐khi ||2167||  

ethā dām̐r̤āiẏā viśvambhara harṣacite |  
viśvarūpe ke cala bhojana karite ||2168||  

ei pathe dhari viśvarūpera vasana |  
ghare cale se adbhuta bhaṅgite gamana ||2169||  

viśvambhara-saṅge viśvarūpa cali yāẏa |  
vāravāra nimāicāndera mukha cāẏa ||2170||  

viśvarūpa kathā ki baliba śrīnivāsa |  
kichudine viśvarūpa karilā sannyāsa ||2171||  

viśvarūpa lāgi bhaktagaṇa eikhāne |  
kahi kata vyākula calite cāhe vane ||2172||  

pāṣaṇḍera vākya-vajrāghāte bhaktagaṇa |  
eikhāne vasi mahāduḥkhe nimagana ||2173||  

ethā śrīadvaitadeva guṇera ālaẏa |  
mahādarpa kari bhaktagaṇe prabodhaẏa ||2174||  

ei gṛhe bhaktagaṇa kare haridhvani |  
dhāiÿā āise viśvambhara tāhā śuni ||2175||  

sabe kahe kene bāpa āilā hethāẏa |  
śuni kahe kibā kārye ḍākilā āmāẏa ||2176||  

eta kahi śiśu-saṅge yāẏa khelāite |  
cinite nāraẏe keha tām̐ra icchāmate ||2177||  

ohe śrīnivāsa, ki baliba eikhāne |  
nimāi par̤ena tā praśaṁse sarvajane ||2178||  

viśvarūpa-sannyāsa-āśaṅkā kari cite |  
viśvambhare pitā niṣbedhilena par̤ite ||2179||  

par̤ite nā pāiẏā nimāira duḥkha mane |  
punaḥ ārambhilena uddhatya śiśusane ||2180||  

e sakala gṛhe nānā upadrava kare |  
krodha kare, keha kichu kahite nā pāre ||2181||  

jagannātha miśra śiṣṭagaṇera kathāẏa |  
par̤ite kahena putre ullāsa hiẏāẏa ||2182||  

par̤aẏe nimāi priẏa śiśugaṇa-sane |  
kare nānā vidyācarcā vasi eikhāne ||2183||  

jagannātha miśra priẏatamera e-ghara |  
nimāira yajñasūtra-kārye se tatpara ||2184||  

ei gaṅgādāsa paṇḍitera bār̤ī haẏa |  
vyākaraṇa par̤e ethā śacīra tanaẏa ||2185||  

dine dine vyākaraṇe haiẏā camatkāra |  
vyākaraṇe karaẏe ṭippanī āpanāra ||2186||  

kṛṣṇānanda śrīkamalakānta murārigupte |  
ethā rahi phām̐ki jijñāsaẏe harṣacite ||2187||  

vidyārase magna haiẏā śrīgaurasundara |  
karaẏe ye kriẏā brahmādira agocara ||2188||  

jāhnavīra ei ghāṭe śiṣyagaṇa saṅge |  
kalakrīdā kari gṛhe cale mahāraṅge ||2189||  

viṣṇupūjā kari tulasīre jala diẏā |  
bhuñjiẏā prasāda rahe ethāi āsiẏā ||2190||  

śāstrera prasaṅga vinā kichui nā bhāẏa |  
parama paṇḍita haiẏā phire nadīẏāẏa ||2191||  

ekadina murāriguptera eikhāne |  
kahe kata tāhe tām̐ra krodha nāhi mane ||2192||  

kare śāstracarcā prabhu bhṛtya duijana |  
anyera kā kathā śuniẏā harṣa devagaṇa ||2193||  

rudra-aṁśa murāri āpanā nāi jāne |  
prabhura vyākhyāẏa mahānanda bārh̤‌e mane ||2194||  

ei dekha, śrīvallabha-ācāryera ghara |  
yām̐ra kanyā lakṣmī, yem̐ho sarvāṁśe sundara ||2195||  

kahite ki vallabha-ācārya bhāgyavān |  
eikhāne kaila viśvambhare kanyādāna ||2196||  

vivāhera pūrve gaṅgātīre ei pathe |  
haila śrīlakṣmīra dekhā viśvambhara sāthe ||2197||  

vanamālī ācāryera ei bār̤ī haẏa |  
lakṣmīra vivāhe yāẏa udyogātiśaẏa ||2198|  

śrīlakṣmīre vivāha kariẏā viśvambhara |  
ei pathe mahāraṅge yāna nija ghara ||2199||  

ethā bahu loka viśvambhare praśaṁsaẏa |  
praśaṁse śacīre yāra ehena tanaẏa ||2200||  

eikhāne rahiẏā prabhura bhakta yata |  
nā ciniẏā nija-prabhu śikṣā dena kata ||2201||  

śrīmukunda paṇḍita rahiẏā eikhāne |  
pakṣa-pratipakṣa bahu kare prabhu-sane ||2202||  

ethā pāṣaṇḍīra vākye krodhayukta haiẏā |  
kahena advaita sabe huṅkāra kariẏā ||2203||  

kichudina pare ei nadīẏā-bhitara |  
dekhibā kṛṣṇere śuni ullāsa antara ||2204||  

ei dekha gopīnātha ācāryera ghara |  
madhye madhye ethā āisena viśvambhara ||2205||  

śrīīśvarapurī kichu dina ethā chilā |  
‘kṛṣṇalīlāmṛta grantha’ ethāi racilā ||2206||  

gadādhara paṇḍite parama sneha kare |  
tām̐ra prema-ceṣṭā dekhi par̤āilā tām̐re ||2207||  

viśvambhara-prati śrīpurīra prīti ati |  
grantha pariśodhana karite kahe niti ||2208||  

viśvambhara samīhā karena atiśaẏa |  
yāhāte tām̐hāra prīti se kārya karaẏa ||2209||  

eikhāne gadādhara paṇḍita-sahite |  
haila śāstracarcā ati kautuka tāhāte ||2210||  

ethā sabe śāstracarcā śuni viśvambhare |  
‘kṛṣṇa bhakti hauka’ bali āśīrvāda kare ||2211||  

eikhāne śrīvāsādi vaiṣṇava sabāre |  
praṇamite kata śikṣā dena viśvambhare ||2212||  

ei dekha śrīmukunda sañjaẏa bhavana |  
ethā śāstracarcā prabhu kare anukṣaṇa ||2213||  

ethāi vāsaẏā vipragaṇa sabe kahe |  
vāẏu adhikāra kaila viśvambhara-dehe ||2214||  

premabhakti-vikāra tāhā keho nāi jāne |  
vāẏu-śānti haila śuni sabe harṣa mane ||2215||  

navadvīpe gaurāṅgera adbhuta vilāsa |  
sabā saha kare sadā hāsiẏā sambhāṣa ||2216||  

kebā nā mohita dekhi śacīra nandane |  
ei pathe cale prabhu nagara bhramaṇe ||2217||  

ei tantuvāẏa-gṛhe prabhu viśvambhara |  
vastra laiẏā parilena śobhā manohara ||2218||  

ei gopagaṇa-gṛhe parama kautuke |  
dadhi dugdha navanīta bhuñje mahāsukhe ||2219||  

ei gandhavaṇikera ghare gaurahari |  
parilena divya gandha anugraha kari ||2220||  

ei mālākāra-ghare par̤uẏāra saṅge |  
pare divyamālā jhalamala kare aṅge ||2221||  

ei tāmbūlīra ghare āsi gaurarāẏa |  
tāmbūla bhakṣaṇa kare ullāsa hiẏāẏa |2222||  

ohe śrīnivāsa, gauracandra gaṇasaṅge |  
navadvīpe bhramaṇa karaẏe mahāraṅge ||2223||  

pūrve madhupure prabhu kariẏā bhramaṇa |  
karilena tṛpta aiche sakalera mana ||2224||  

śaṅkhavaṇikera ei bhavane āsiẏā |  
laïlena śaṅkha ati kautuka kariẏā ||2225||  

navadvīpa-madhye ei sarvatra ghara |  
ethā āilena prabhu śacīra kumāra ||2226||  

sumadhura vākye prabhu kahe sarvajñere |  
anya janme ke chilāma kaha dekhi more ||2227||  

śuni jape sarvajña gopāla-mantrabare |  
mantrabale dekhe vāsudevera kumāre ||2228||  

śaṅkha-cakra-gadā padma caturbhuja dekhi |  
cāhi viśvambhara pāne punaḥ mude ām̐khi ||2229||  

punaḥ dekhe nandera nandana vaṁśīdhara |  
tribhaṅga-bhaṅgimā divya śyāmala sundara ||2230||  

śrīrāma-varāha-nṛsiṁhādi-avatāra |  
dekhiẏā sarvajña cinte citre anivāra ||2231||  

prabhu kahe—‘kaha śuna, sarvajña kahaẏa |  
kahila paścāt ebe karaha vijaẏa’ ||2232||  

śuni manda manda hāsi śrīgaurasundara |  
āila ethāẏa ei śrīdharera ghara ||2233||  

śrīdharera saṅge prabhu yata raṅga kare |  
eka mukhe tāhā keho kahite nā pāre ||2234||  

navadvīpa bhramaṇa kariẏā viśvambhara |  
sabā saha ei pathe golā nija-ghara ||2235||  

yuddhakāma-līlā ādi vacanera dūra |  
se saba karena sabe ye icchā prabhura ||2236||  

ei rājapathe prabhu śacīra nandana |  
bhuvanamohana veśe karaẏe bhramaṇa ||2237||  

akasmāt śrīvāsa paṇḍita-sane dekhā |  
tām̐ra sane yata kathā nāhi tāra lekhā ||2238||  

ohe śrīnivāsa, ethā bali gauracandra |  
dekhaẏe gaṅgāra śobhā haïẏā ānanda ||2239||  

caturdike śiṣyavarga, śobhā atiśaẏa |  
kare śāstracarcā prabhu sabhāre mohaẏa ||2240||  

śiṣyagaṇa-madhye keho prabhu viśvambhare |  
dvigvijaẏī-prasaṅga kahaẏa dhīre dhīre ||2241||  

sarasvatī devī vaktā tāhāra jihvāẏa |  
sarvatra kariẏā jaẏa āilā nadīẏāẏa ||2242||  

vidyābale digvijaẏī kāhuke nā gaṇe |  
hastī aśva dolā bahu loka tām̐ra sane ||2243||  

navadvīpe bar̤a bar̤a adhyāpakagaṇa |  
haïla sabhāra ati cintayukta mana ||2244||  

śuni manda manda hāsi kahe viśvambhara |  
ahaṅkāra kāru nāhi rākhena īśvara ||2245||  

dūre rahi digvijaẏī śobhā nirakhiẏā |  
āilā nikaṭe ati vismita haïẏā ||2246||  

viśvambhara atyanta gaurava kari pare |  
kahilena gaṅgāra māhātmya varṇivāre ||2247||  

digvijaẏī mahādarpe bahu śloka kaila |  
viśvambhara tāre vyākhyā karite balila ||2248||  

ati se kaṭhina śloka kāru gamya nahe |  
hāsi digvijaẏī nija-śloka-artha kahe ||2249||  

śloka artha kari vipra hailā avasara |  
śloka-ādi-madhye-ante doṣe viśvambhara ||2250||  

digvijaẏī parābhava haïẏā cintaẏa |  
tathāpi gaurava rākhe śacīra tanaẏa ||2251||  

pūrṇabrahma sanātana prabhu gaurarāẏa |  
hena jñāna haila sarasvatīra kṛpāẏa ||2252||  

digvijaẏī prabhupade laïla śaraṇa |  
ye kṛpā karila prabhu nā haẏa varṇana ||2253||  

dvagvijaẏī vaiṣṇava-sampradāẏa-madhye haẏa |  
keśava-kāśmīra nāma diẏe paricaẏa ||2254||  

śrīnārāẏaṇera śiṣya haṁsa e pracāra |  
sanakādi catuḥsana hana śiṣya tām̐ra ||2255||  

sanakera śiṣya śrīnārada mahāśaẏa |  
tām̐ra śiṣya nimbāditā guṇera ālaẏa ||2256||  

śrīnimbādityera śiṣyācārya śrīnivāsa |  
haïla sarvatra yām̐ra mahimā prakāśa ||2257||  

tām̐ra śiṣya viśvācārya sarvāṁśe pradhāna |  
tām̐ra śrīpuruṣottamācārya vidyāvān ||2258||  

śrīvilāsācārya tām̐ra śiṣya mahādhīra |  
tām̐ra śiṣya śrīsvarūpa ācārya gabhīra ||2259||  

tām̐ra priẏa śiṣya śrīmādhavācāryavarya |  
tām̐ra priẏa śiṣya śrīmadvallabhadrācārya ||2260||  

tām̐ra śiṣya padmācārya sarvatra vidita |  
tām̐ra śiṣya śrīśyāma ācārya cāru rīta ||2261||  

tām̐ra priẏaśiṣya hana ācārya gopāla |  
tām̐ra śiṣya kṛpācārya parama daẏāla ||2262||  

tām̐ra śiṣya devācārya guṇera ālaẏa |  
tām̐ra śiṣya śrīsundara bhaṭṭa daẏāmaẏa ||2263||  

śrīmat padmanābha bhaṭṭa śiṣya hana tām̐ra |  
tām̐ra śiṣya upendra bhaṭṭa khyāti yām̐ra ||2264||  

tām̐ra priẏa śiṣya rāmacandra bhaṭṭa hana |  
tām̐ra śiṣya sarvapriẏa śrībhaṭṭa vāmana ||2265||  

tām̐ra śiṣya kṛṣṇabhaṭṭa parama suśānta |  
tām̐ra śiṣya padmākara bhaṭṭa vidyāvanta ||2266||  

śrīpadmākarera śiṣya bhaṭṭa śrīśravaṇa |  
tām̐ra śiṣya bhūribhaṭṭa ceṣṭā vilakṣaṇa ||2267||  

tām̐ra ati priẏa śiṣya bhaṭṭa śrīmādhava |  
tām̐ra śiṣya śyāmabhaṭṭa mahā anubhava ||2268||  

tām̐ra śiṣya śrīgopāla bhaṭṭa sucarita |  
tām̐ra śiṣya balabhadra bhaṭṭa śuddharīta ||2269||  

tām̐ra śiṣya gopīnātha bhaṭṭa sarvapūjya |  
tām̐ra śiṣya śrīkeśava bhaṭṭa ceṣṭāścarya ||2270||  

tām̐ra śiṣya śrīgokula bhaṭṭa mahādhīra |  
tām̐ra ati priẏa śiṣya keśava kāśmīra ||2271||  

sarasvatīdevīra kariẏā mantra-japa |  
haila sarvavidyā-sphūṛti bār̤ila pratāpa ||2272||  

sarva digvijaẏa kari ‘digvijaẏī’ khyāti |  
kāśmīra deśastha ati śiṣṭa viprajāti ||2273||  

ati śubhakṣaṇe navadvīpete āilā |  
saba tyāga kari prabhu-ājñāẏa calilā ||2274||  

keśava-kāśmīra digvijaẏī lajjā ithe |  
varṇi līlābhoga ‘laghukeśava’ nāmete ||2275||  

digvijaẏī keśava kāśmīra bhāgyavanta |  
ḍubilena ye sukhe kahite nāi anta ||2276||  

nimāi sthāne digvijaẏī parājaẏa |  
sarvatra vidita loke e yaśa ghoṣaẏa ||2277||  

yekhāne sekhāne mātra ei kathā śuni |  
nimāi paṇḍita adhyāpaka-śiromaṇi ||2278||  

ei mata nānā raṅga kare gaṅgātīre |  
svecchāmaẏa prabhu ei pathe yāna ghare ||2279||  

ekadina ei pathe karite gamana |  
dekhaẏe sannyāsī āisena viśajana ||2280||  

parama ādare se sakala sannyāsīre |  
vividha sāmagrī bhuñjāẏena laiẏā ghare ||2281|  

aiche sadā sannyāsīre karāna bhojana |  
sabe mahā-vismita nā dekhe upārjana ||2282||  

baṅgadeśe yāite prabhura icchā haila |  
yātrā kari ei vipragṛhe sthiti kaila ||2283||  

śiṣyagaṇa-saṅge prabhu baṅgadeśe giẏā |  
śrītapana miśre dila kāśī pāṭhāiẏā ||2284||  

baṅga dhanya kari āilena kathe dine |  
āgulari vipragaṇa ei pathe āne ||2285||  

śiṣyavarga veṣṭita śrīgaurāṅgasundara |  
sarvacitta mohiẏā calena nija-ghara ||2286||  

ethā vasi vipragaṇa adhairya antare |  
lakṣmīra viẏoga-kathā kahe dhīre dhīre ||2287||  

viśvambhara āilena baṅgadeśa haïte |  
gṛha śūnya dekhi mahā-duḥkha pābe cite ||2288||  

nimāi paṇḍita mahāpuruṣa ratana |  
eta kahi prabodhite gelā sarvajana ||2289||  

ekadina ethā keho snāna kari āilā |  
nā dekhi tilaka, karibāre śikṣā dilā ||2290||  

ohe śrīnivāsa, ethā nimāi raṅgete |  
baṅgadeśī loke kadarthena nānā mate ||2291||  

ethā viśvambhara ye ye raṅga parakāśe |  
kahite se saba kathā mukhe nā āise ||2292||  

ei dekha sanātana miśrera bhavana |  
yem̐ha rājapaṇḍita sarvāṁśe vilakṣaṇa ||2293||  

sanātanamiśrera duhitā viṣṇupriẏā |  
eka mukhe kahite nā pāri tām̐ra kriẏā ||2294||  

sanātana miśra mahā ānandita mane |  
viśvambhare kanyā dāna kaila eikhāne ||2295||  

dekha kāśīnātha paṇḍitera vāsasthāna |  
viṣṇupriẏā-vivāhe udyoga ati tāna ||2296||  

ethā bhaktagaṇa mahā-duḥkhita haïẏā |  
karena ākṣepa bhaktasaṅga nā pāiẏā ||2297||  

‘hā kṛṣṇa, hā kṛṣṇa’ bali chār̤e dīrgha-śvāsa |  
hena kāle āilā ṭhākura haridāsa ||2298||  

haridāsa ṭhākurera adbhuta carita |  
kahiba kateka tāhā sarvatra vidita ||2299||  

ethā gauracandra vasi vicāraẏe cite |  
mora avatāra premabhakti prakāśite ||2300||  

gaẏā haite āsi bhakta-duḥkha vināśiba |  
parama durlabha premabhakti prakāśiba ||2301||  

eta vicāriẏā prabhu ullāsa antare |  
māẏe prabodhiẏā cale gaẏā karibāre ||2302|  

ei vipra-ghare yātrā kariẏā rahilā |  
prātaḥkāle śiyyasaṅge e pathe calilā ||2303||  

gaẏā kari viśvambhara īśvarapurīre |  
yata anugraha tāhā ke kahite pāre ||2304||  

tathā premabhakti prakāśāranta haïla |  
śiṣyagaṇa-saṅge navadvīpe yātrā kaila ||29305||  

navadvīpe āilena śrīśacīkumāra |  
navadvīpe haila mahā ānanda sabhāra ||2306||  

āgusari ānite gelena sarvajana |  
ei pathe prabhu gṛhe karilā gamana ||2307||  

premabhakti-rase sām̐tāraẏe gaurarāẏa |  
dekhi sarva vaiṣṇavera ullāsa hiẏāẏa ||2308||  

śrīvāsa rāmaï gopīnātha gadādhare |  
ethā harṣe śrīmān kahaẏe se sabhāre ||2309||  

gaẏā haite āilena paṇḍita nimāi |  
se sakala auddhatyera leśamātra nāi ||2310||  

gaẏātīrtha-prasaṅga kahiẏā mo sabhāre |  
viṣṇupādapadma-kathā kahite nā pāre ||2311||  

nadīra pravāha prāẏa jhare dunaẏana |  
kṛṣṇa bali bhūme par̤e haiẏā acetana ||2312||  

dekhinu adbhuta tām̐ra premera vikāra |  
śuni kata kahe mahā ullāsa sabhāra ||2313||  

ethā śrīvāsādi praśaṁsiẏā viśvambhare |  
gaṅgātīre baise giẏā śuklāmbara-ghare ||2314||  

ei śuklāmbara brahmacārīra bhavana |  
gaẏā haite āsi ethā prabhura gamana ||2315||  

śrīmān paṇḍita ādi ethāẏa dekhiẏā |  
kahite kṛṣṇera kathā uthalaẏe hiẏā ||2316||  

āpanā māniẏā dīna śacīra nandana |  
dhariẏā sabhāra galā karaẏe krandana ||2317||  

gopyarūpe ye ye bhakta chilena yathāẏā |  
kām̐daẏe sakale, gauracandrera premāẏa ||2318||  

prabhu kahe—‘ke kām̐daẏe gharera bhitara’ |  
śuklāmbara kahaẏe—‘tomāra gadādhara’ ||2319||  

haila premārambha yaiche kahite nā pāri |  
ḍubilena ānanda-samudre brahmacārī ||2320||  

ratnagarbha ācārya e-vṛkṣa-sannidhāne |  
par̤e bhāgavata-padya mahānanda-mane ||2321||  

śuni gauracandra nija-bhaktira bar̤āi |  
mūrchita haïẏā prāme par̤aẏe ethāi ||2322||  

śrīratnagarbhera bhāgya kahite nārila |  
cetana pāiẏā prabhu tāre āliṅgila ||2323||  

ohe śrīnivāsa, ki baliba eikhāne |  
āpanā prakāśe prabhu āpana-kīrtane ||2324||  

dekhi viśvambhara-premāveśa bhaktagaṇa |  
ethā śrīadvaite saba kaila nivedana ||2325||  

sarvatattvajñātā prabhu advaita-īśvara |  
śuni ati ullāse pulaka kalevara ||2326||  

bhaktagaṇe aneka prakāre jānāilā |  
dekhilena sbapne yāhā tāhāo kahilā ||2327||  

advaitacandrera ceṣṭā bujhe kon jana |  
kṣaṇe prakāśaẏe kṣaṇe karaẏe gopana ||2328||  

śuniẏā apūrva kathā advaitera sthāne |  
calilena bhaktagaṇa praṇami tāhāne ||2329||  

ohe śrīnivāsa, gauracandrera carita |  
dine dine nadīẏāẏa haïla vidita ||2330||  

gaṅgāra e ghāṭe prabhu māti bhaktirase |  
karaẏe bhaktera sevā aśeṣa-viśeṣe ||2331||  

prakāśe ye dainya tāhā kahite nā pāri |  
bhaktasevā mukhya jānāẏena gaurahari ||2332||  

ki baliba prabhura e mane bar̤a sādha |  
nirantara laïte bhaktera āśīrvāda ||2333||  

gur̤harūpe prabhu vilasaẏe nadīẏāẏa |  
ke jānite pāre prabhu yadi nā jānāẏa ||2334||  

sarvapūjya haïẏāo paṇḍita nimāi |  
vaiṣṇavera sāji dhuti bahe lajjā nāi ||2335||  

ethā bhaktagaṇa gauracandra-mukha heri |  
kare āśīrvāda kata upadeśa kari ||2336||  

bhaktapadadhūli viśvambhara laiẏā śire |  
kahena yateka tāhā ke kahite pāre ||2337||  

ekadina ei pathe prabhu viśvambhara |  
advaita-vāsāẏa gelā saṅge gadādhara ||2338||  

dekhiẏā advaita ethā premāẏa vihvala |  
saghane sonāra aṅga kare ṭalamala ||2339||  

advaita ācārya mahā ullāsa antare |  
kahi kata prabhura pūjāra sajja kare ||2340||  

gandhapuṣpa diẏā pūje prabhura caraṇa |  
vāravāra praṇamiẏā karaẏe stavana ||2341||  

advaitera kriẏā dekhi gadādhara hāse |  
dante jihvā daṁśiẏā kahaẏe mṛdu bhāṣe ||2342||  

anugraha karibe maṅgala yāte haẏa |  
bālake kaha aiche e ucita naẏa ||2343||  

hāsiẏā advaita kahe nā jāna ekhane |  
e bālaka ye hena jānibe kichu dine ||2344||  

śuni gadādhara-citte haïla vismaẏa |  
mane mane guṇe e īśvara suniścaẏa ||2345||  

katakṣaṇa bāhya prakāśiẏā gaurarāẏa |  
advaitere kahi kata āpanā lukāẏa ||2346||  

advaitera premādhīna prabhu gaurahari |  
haila ye kautuka ethā kahite nā pāri ||2347||  

kata abhilāṣa kari ullāsa antare |  
ethā haite advaita gelena śāntipure |2348||  

ethā saṁkīīrtanāveśe prabhura ye sukha |  
se āveśa varṇite nā jāne caturmukha ||2349||  

vaiṣṇavasakala preme sthira haite nāre |  
ghucila manuṣyajñāna prabhu viśvambhare ||2350||  

ethā premāveśe prabhu vaiṣṇave kahila |  
kānāira nāṭyaśālā-grāme ye dekhila ||2351||  

ethā saṁkīrtane kare huṅkāra-garjana |  
balpiẏā maraẏe śuni pāṣaṇḍīra gaṇa ||2352||  

pāṣaṇḍera vākye vaiṣṇavera duḥkha haẏa |  
prabhu avatīrṇa tāhā keho nā jānaẏa ||2353||  

duḥkha vināśite jñānāite āpanāẏa |  
parama sundaraveśe bhrame nadīẏāẏa ||2354||  

ghare haite ei pathe āise sājiẏā |  
dekhiẏā pāṣaṇḍigaṇa maraẏe balpiẏā ||2355||  

śrīgaurasundarera nadīẏā bhramaṇalīlā—  
dekhi gauracandra-śobhā bhuvanamohana |  
sukṛtigaṇera mahā ullasita mana ||2356||  

ki nārī puruṣa sabhe adhairya antara |  
dekhi gauracandra kata kahe paraspara ||2357||  

gīte yathā—kāmoda—  

gaura-vidhuvara,		varajamohana,  
bhramaṇa karu nadīẏāẏa |  
vṛddha puruṣa,		asaṁkhya patha gata |  
nirikhe haraṣa hiẏāẏa ||2358||  

keu kahe kiẏe,		anaṅga sugaṭhana,  
kone sirajala kela |  
aiche aparūpa,		rūpaka bahula,  
naẏanagocara bhela ||2359||  

kou kaha kiẏe,		neha ghaṭaï ki,  
kahaba kahaï nā yāẏa |  
hṛdaẏa-sampuṭe,		dharava anukṣaṇa,  
kaha ki karaba upāẏa ? ||2360||  

kou kata kata,		bhāti bhāla ani-  
vāra āśīṣa deta |  
dāsa narahari,		pāhuṅka mādhurī,  
nirata diṭhi bhari leta ||2361||  

kāmoda—  

āju ki ānanda nadīẏāẏa |  
pathe yata vṛddha nārī,		dām̐r̤āiẏā sāri sāri,  
śacīra dulāla pāne cāẏa || dhrru ||2362||  

keho kāru prati kaẏa, e kabhu mānuṣa naẏa,  
bujhilāma cite vicāriẏā |  
emana bālaka yena,		nā dekhi nā śuni hena,  
bhārata bhūmete janamiẏā ||2363||  

keha punaḥ punaḥ bhaṇe,	ki baliba etadine,  
haïla sakala duḥkha-nāśa |  
keho kahe mane yāhā		kahite nāriẏe tāhā,  
dhanya ei nadīẏāra vāsa ||2364||  

keha kahe śacī dhanya,		karila kateka puṇya,  
kahite nā jāni śneha tām̐ra |  
e cām̐da-vadane yāke,		sadā mā baliẏā ḍāke,  
hena bhāgya āche āra kāra ||2365||  

keho kahe ei mate,		ber̤‌āuka nadīẏāte,  
sakala sukṛti-saṅge laiẏā |  
keho kahe mane hena,		sonāra nimāi yena,  
kakhana nā chār̤aẏe nadīẏā ||2366||  

keho kahe nadīẏāte,		sadā rahu kuśalete,  
vidhire prārthanā ei kari |  
narahari-prāṇa gorā,		kevala ām̐khera tārā,  
ihāra bālāi laiẏā mari ||2367||  

bhūpālī—  

gaurāṅga-gamana,		śuni andhagaṇa,  
bāhire bārh̤‌āẏa pā |  
cāhe ghana ghana,		pāiẏā naẏana,  
ulase bharaẏe gā ||2368||  

keho kāru kare,		dhari kahe dhīre,  
āju se saphala haila |  
dite mahānanda,		vidhi kaile andha,  
āne nā dekhite dila ||2369||  

e rūpa amiẏā,		piẏā enā hiẏā,  
ki kare nā yāẏa jānā |  
hena rūpa yeha,		nā dekhila seha,  
naẏana thākite kāṇā ||2370||  

sadā dekhibāre,		dhāẏa vāre vāre  
ām̐khi nā dhairaya bām̐dhe |  
narahari sākhi,		saum̐pilu e ām̐khi,  
sonāra nimāicānde ||2371||  

tor̤ī—  

nadīẏā bhramaẏe,		gorā guṇamaṇi,  
śuni paṅgu pathe giẏā |  
animiṣa ām̐khi		se mukha nirakhi,  
ānande uthale hiẏā ||2372||  

keho kahe śuna,		vidhi sakaruṇa,  
ebe se bujhilu mane |  
ye lāgiẏā paṅgu		karile se phala,  
phalāle eteka dine ||2373||  

paṅgu nā haïle,		gṛha-kāja-chale,  
yāitāma dūra deśa |  
nā jāniẏe tathā,		maraṇa haïle,  
duḥkhera nahita śeṣa ||2374||  

paṅgu haiẏā yena,		thāki mena hena,  
vidhire prārthanā kari |  
narahari nāthe,		sadā nadīẏāte,  
dekhi e naẏana bhari ||2375||  

kāmoda—  

bhuvanamohana,		gorāguṇamaṇi,  
rājapathe kata bhaṅgite cale |  
kata kata śata,		madana murachi,  
loṭāẏa caraṇa-kamala-tale ||2376||  

cāridike loka,		kare dhāẏā dhāi,  
atula śobhāẏa mohita haiẏā |  
tanu mana prāṇa,		kebā nāhi nichaẏe,  
paraspara cāru-carita kaiẏā ||2377||  

nadīẏā-nagare,		nāgarāli-veśe,  
phiraẏe navīna nāgara yata |  
goracānda-pāne,		cāhi tā sabhāra,  
nāgara-garaba haila hata ||2378||  

jagatera mājhe,		pravīṇatā ati,  
rasikatā-made vibhora phārā |  
narahari bhaṇe,		khadyota yemana,  
vidhu āge haila temani tārā ||2379||  

dhānaśī—  

nadīẏāra śaśī,		raṅge rājapathe,  
hili duli cale pulaka hiẏā |  
alakhita yata,		yuvatī athira,  
sāthe ādha diṭhi se aṅge diẏā ||2380||  

keho kahe dekha,		dekha sakhī ei,  
gorārūpa kiẏe amiẏārāśi |  
tāmbūlera rāge,		adhara ujjvala,  
tāhe kibā manda madhura hāsi ||2381||  

raṅgaṇa phulera,		mālā dole kibā,  
ām̐khera bhaṅgite bhuvana mohe |  
cām̐cara cikura-		caẏa cāru kibā,  
kapāle candana-tilaka śohe ||2382||  

kibā jānu bhuja-		yugera balani,  
parisara buke kebā nā bhule |  
narahari pam̐hu,		rase sumajilu,  
dilu tilāñjali e lāja kule ||2383||  

ohe śrīnivāsa, prabhu nadīẏā-bhamaṇe |  
āpanā prakāśe sukha dite bhaktagaṇe ||2384||  

gamana bhaṅgite caturdika nirikhaẏa |  
dekhāẏe gogaṇa gaṅgā-puline śobhaẏa ||2385||  

hāmbā-raba kari yuthe yuthe dhenu yāẏa |  
piẏe bāri ūrdhva pucche caturdike cāẏa ||2386||  

paraspara kare yuddha prabhu tā dekhiẏā |  
‘mui sei, mui sei’ balaẏe garjiẏā ||2387||  

adbhuta āveśe ei pathe viśvambhara |  
dhāiẏā gelena harṣe śrīvāsera ghara ||2388||  

śrīvāsa-bhavane ei ghare dvāra diẏā |  
pūjaẏe nṛsiṁhadeve nimagna haïẏā ||2389||  

kare padāghāta gauracandre ei dvāre |  
śrīvāsera dhyāna-bhaṅga haila se huṅkāre ||2390||  

dhyana-bhaṅga krodhe vipra cāhe cāri pāne |  
dekhe tejomaẏa viśvambhare vīrāsane ||2391||  

śaṅkha-catra-gadā-pada cāri hāte laiẏā |  
karaẏe garjana kata śrīvāsere kaiẏa ||2392||  

śrīvāsa trāsete stabdha kichui nā sphure |  
prabhura ājñāẏa harṣa haiẏā stuti kare ||2393||  

śrīmanmahāprabhura īśvaryadarśane śrīvāsera stuti—  

prabhura adbhuta kriẏā ye ye avatāre |  
tāhā prakāśaẏe se āveśe stuti-dvāre ||2394||  

sarvaśāstre paṇḍita śrīvāsa mahāśaẏa |  
prabhu āge kare stuti uthale hṛdaẏa ||2395||  

śuniẏā adbhuta stuti-bhaṅgi gaurahari |  
dilena svābhīṣṭa, vara anugraha kari ||2396||  

goṣṭhīsaha śrīvāsa-bhāgyerā sīmā nāi |  
prabhura caraṇa pūje śrīvāsa ethāi ||2397||  

se adbhuta pūjāra tulanā nāi dite |  
pūjāẏa prasanna yata ke pāre kahite ||2398||  

sadbhāra mastake cāru caraṇa arpaẏe |  
parama ānande bhaktabhaẏa vināśaẏe ||2399||  

nārāẏaṇī nāme eka bālikā ethāẏa |  
kṛṣṇa bali kānde tem̐ho prabhura ājñāẏa ||2400||  

se bālikā śrīvāsera bhrātṛsutā haẏa |  
cāri vatsarera kanyā saubhāgyātiśaẏa ||2401||  

prabhu bhāvāveśa yata anya-agocara |  
bāhya pāi lajjāyukta hana viśvambhara ||2402||  

‘kāhu nā kahiba’ ihā kahi śrīvāsere |  
ethā haite e-pathe gelena nija-ghare ||2403||  

varāhabhāve prabhura murāri-gṛhe gamana—  

ekadina prabhu śrīvarāha-bhāvāveśe |  
garjiẏā e pathe cale murāri-āvāse |2404||  

ei viṣṇumandire praveśi viśvambhara |  
varāha-ākāra hailā parama sundara ||2405||  

jalapātra gār̤u ethā sammukhe dekhiẏā |  
dharilena dante svānubhāve magna haiẏā ||2406||  

murārira prati prabhu kahe vāravāra |  
‘etadina nā jānaha mora avatāra’ ||2407||  

haïlā murāri stabdha prabhura darśane |  
ki baliba kichui nā sphuraẏe vaẏane ||2408||  

bola bola bale prabhu kichu nāi bhaẏa |  
murāri karaẏe stuti netre dhārā vaẏa ||2409|  

murārira stuti śuni prabhu gaurahari |  
bhāvāveśe kahe yata kahite nā pāri ||2410||  

yata anugraha prabhu kailā murārire |  
murārira ye ānanda kahite ke pāre ||2411||  

ei mata prabhu sarva bhaktera vāsāẏa |  
mahā anugraha kari āpanā jānāẏa ||2412||  

āpanāra prabhu bhakta cini harṣamane |  
kare saṁkīrtana pāṣaṇḍīre nāi gaṇe ||2413||  

ekadina śrīvāsa-murāri āsi hethā |  
paraspara kahe gauracandrera guṇagāthā ||2414||  

śrīvāsa paṇḍita khede kahe vāravāra |  
‘etadina nā cinilu prabhu āpanāra’ ||2415||  

sadāi vidare hiẏā kahite ki āra |  
hena prabhu sāji dhuti bahila āmāra ||2416||  

‘kṛṣṇa bhakti hauka bali āśīrvāda kainu |  
kṛṣṇe kṛṣṇa bhajibāre kata śikṣā dinu’ ||2417||  

aiche śrīmurāri ādi prabhupriẏagaṇa |  
kari kata kheda sabhe karaẏe krandana ||2418||  

śrīnityānanda prabhura nadīẏāẏa āgamana—  

ethā prabhu śrīvāsādi sakala bhaktere |  
nityānanda-gamana jānāna ṭhāre ṭhāre ||2419||  

akasmāt nityānanda āsi nadīẏāẏa |  
rahilena gupte tā jānilā gaurarāẏa ||2420||  

nityānanda anya agocara jānāiẏā |  
tām̐re milibāre cale ei patha diẏā ||2421||  

śrīnandana-ācārya parama bhāgyavān |  
dekha śrīnivāsa, ei bhavana tām̐hāna ||2422||  

bhaktagoṣṭhī saha prabhu giẏā e-bhavane |  
dekhe nityānanda vasi āchaẏe dheẏāne ||2423||  

nirupama nityānanda-aṅgera mādhurī |  
dām̐r̤āiẏā bhaktagaṇa dekhe netra bhari ||2424||  

nityānanda-sammukhe vilase viśvambhara |  
nityānanda dekhe prabhu śobhā manohara ||2425|  

tathāhi śrīcaitanyabhāgavate—  
viśvambhara-mūrti yena madana-samāna |  
divya gandhamālya divya vāsa-paridhāna ||2426||  

ki haẏa kanaka-dyuti se dehera āge |  
se vadana cāhite cāndera sādha lāge ||2427||  

se danta dekhite hare mukutāra māna |  
se veśa-bandhana dekhe nā rahe geẏāna ||2428||  

dekhite ārakta sei aruṇa-naẏana |  
āra ki kamala āche hena laẏa jñāna ||2429||  

se ājānu bhuja dui hṛdaẏa supīna |  
tathi śobhe śukla yajñasūtra ati kṣīṇa ||2430||  

lalāṭe vicitra ūrdhvatilaka sundara |  
ābharaṇa vine sarva aṅga manohara ||2431||  

kibā haẏa koṭi maṇi se natha cāhite |  
se hāsa dekhite kibā karibe amṛte ||2432||  

viśvambhara-śobhā dekhi nityānanda rāẏa |  
kahite ki jāni yaiche ullāsa-hiẏāẏa ||2433||  

nityānandacandrera antara prakāśite |  
śrīvāsa par̤ila śloka prabhura iṅgite ||2434||  

tathāhi śrīmadbhāgavate daśama skandhe (21.5)—  
barhāpīr̤aṁ naṭavaravapuḥ karṇaẏoḥ karṇikāraṁ  
vibhradvāsaḥ kanakakapiśaṁ vaijaẏastīñca mālām |  
randhrān veṇoradharasudhayā puraẏan gopavṛndair-  
vṛndāraṇyaṁ svapadaramaṇaṁ prāviśadgītakīrtiḥ ||2435||  

kṛṣṇadhyāna-śloka śuni nityānanda rāẏa |  
se bhāva-āveśa tāhā kebā nāi gāẏa ||2436||  

gīte yathā—māẏūra—  

bhāve gara gara,		nitāi sundara,  
heri gorā-mukhacāndera chaṭā |  
kata uṭhe cite,		nāre thira haite,  
prati aṅga nava pulaka-ghaṭā ||2437||  

kibā unamāda,		khena siṁhanāda,  
khene loṭāyaẏe dharaṇītale |  
khene dīrghaśvāsa,	khene mahā-hāsa,  
khase vāsa bhāse ām̐khera jale ||2438||  

khene yor̤a lampha,	khene dehe kampa,  
khene dhāẏa keu dharite nāre |  
khene kibā kaiẏā,		rahe thira haiẏā,  
sāmāiẏā viśvambhara kore ||2439||  

nityānande kole,		laiẏā netra-jale,  
bhāse kibā pam̐hu premera rīti |  
kahe narahari,		śrīvāsādi cāri-  
pāśe kānde keu nā dhare dhṛti ||2440||  

ohe śrīnivāsa, ethā ānanda aśeṣa |  
bhuvane vidita nityānanda-bhāvāveśa ||2441||  

ethā viśvambhara-kole rahe nityānanda |  
tāhā dekhi gadādhara hāse manda manda ||2442||  

prabhu viśvambhara nityānanda rahi ethā |  
kahite nā jāni dom̐he kahila ye kathā ||2443||  

śrīvāsādi bhakta ethā bhāsila ye sukhe |  
se saba kahite nā āise eka mukhe ||2444||  

ethā nityānande kahe śacīra kumāra |  
‘kāli paurṇamāsī vyāsapūjana tomāra’ ||2445||  

kothā pūjā habe śuni ullāsa antare |  
hāsi kahe—‘e śrīvāsa vāmanāra ghare’ ||2446||  

nityānanda-vākye ethā harṣa viśvambhara |  
śrīvāsa-sahite kathā haïla vistara ||2447||  

sakalei nandanācāryera gṛha haite |  
śrīvāsapaṇḍita-ghare gelā ei pathe ||2448||  

śrīvāsa gṛhe śrīmanmahāprabhura vividha līlā—  

ohe śrīnivāsa, ei śrīvāsa-aṅgane |  
nāce gauracandra nityānanda-saṅkīrtane ||2449||  

dui prabhu nāce caturdike bhaktagaṇa |  
ye prema-āveśa tāhā nā haẏa varṇana ||2450||  

balarāma-āveśe ethāi gaurahari |  
nityānandacandre prakāśaẏe bhakti kari ||2451||  

lāpha diẏā uṭhe prabhu khaṭṭāra upara |  
‘vāruṇī vāruṇī’ bali ḍāke nirantara ||2452||  

keho pātra bhari gaṅgājala dila āni |  
sabhe dekhe prabhu yena piẏe kādambinī ||2453||  

śrīhala muṣala māge nityānanda-sthāne |  
dila nityānanda tā dekhila bhāgyavāne ||2454||  

ethā harṣe prabhu padmāvatīra nandana |  
śrīgauracandrera kaila yar̤abhuja-darśana ||2455||  

ethā prabhu ‘nār̤ā nār̤ā’ bali ḍāka dila |  
nār̤ā-śabde advaita ācārye jānāila ||2456||  

premānanda magna haiẏā kata kathā kaẏa |  
śuni bhaktagaṇera ullāsa atiśaẏa ||2457||  

ethā nityānanda preme haïlā vihvala |  
kothā vā rahila tām̐ra daṇḍa-kamaṇḍala ||2458||  

bālyāveśe sadāi cañcala nityānanda |  
karaẏe susthira tām̐re dhari gauracandra ||2459||  

ethā rātre nityānanda kahi kibā kathā |  
daṇḍa-kamaṇḍalu bhāṅgi phelāilā ethā ||2460||  

prabhu viśvambhara daṇḍa-kamaṇḍalu laiẏā |  
samarpila gaṅgāẏa nā jāni kibā kaiẏā ||2461||  

nityānande laiẏā snāna karilā gaṅgāẏa |  
tathā ye kautuka tāhā kahā nāhi yāẏa ||2462||  

śrīvyāsa pūjā—  

gandha-candanādi laiẏā vividha vidhāne |  
vyāsapūjārambha prabhu kailā eikhāne ||2463||  

yaiche vyāsapūjā tāhā kahite nā pāri |  
vyāsapūjā-kautuka dekhinu netra bhari ||2464||  

eikhāne jagat-jananī śacī āi |  
sama snehāviṣṭa dekhi nimāi nitāi ||2465||  

vyāsapūjā-saṅkīrtane ye bhāvavikāra |  
se saba bhāvite hiẏā vidar āmāra ||2466||  

vyāsapūjā-naivedya-bhakṣaṇa eikhāne |  
tāhe ye kautuka tā kahite kebā jāne ||2467||  

ethā chila kunda puṣpavṛkṣa śobhāmaẏa |  
puṣpa-caẏanete vaiṣṇavānandātiśaẏā ||2468||  

ohe śrīnivāsa, ekadina gaurārāẏa |  
nijagṛha haite śīghra āilā hethāẏa ||2469||  

śrīvāsera prati prabhu kahena hāsiẏā |  
advaita āise mora pūjāsajja laiẏā ||2470||  

mora ṭhākurāli dekhibāre icchā tāra |  
eta kahi premāveśe karaẏe huṅkāra ||2471||  

ohe śrīnivāsa, ethā haite gaurarāẏa |  
e viṣṇu-maṇḍape baise viṣṇura khaṭṭāẏa ||2472||
